     1	import time
     2	
     3	import requests
     4	
     5	
     6	DDF_PROPERTIES_URL = "https://ddfapi.realtor.ca/odata/v1/Property"
     7	
     8	
     9	def fetch_all_properties(
    10	    headers,
    11	    filter_expression=None,
    12	    max_pages=0,
    13	    progress_callback=None,
    14	):
    15	    """
    16	    Download property pages from the DDF API.
    17	
    18	    Returns:
    19	        tuple[list[dict], int]:
    20	        - downloaded property records
    21	        - number of downloaded pages
    22	    """
    23	    params = {
    24	        "$top": 100,
    25	        "$orderby": "ModificationTimestamp desc",
    26	    }
    27	
    28	    if filter_expression:
    29	        params["$filter"] = filter_expression
    30	
    31	    all_properties = []
    32	    url = DDF_PROPERTIES_URL
    33	    page_count = 0
    34	    page_limit = max(0, int(max_pages or 0))
    35	    download_started_at = time.monotonic()
    36	
    37	    while url and (
    38	        page_limit == 0 or page_count < page_limit
    39	    ):
    40	        next_page_number = page_count + 1
    41	        total_elapsed = (
    42	            time.monotonic() - download_started_at
    43	        )
    44	
    45	        if progress_callback:
    46	            progress_callback(
    47	                f"Requesting DDF page {next_page_number:,}... "
    48	                f"{len(all_properties):,} listings downloaded | "
    49	                f"elapsed {total_elapsed:.1f}s"
    50	            )
    51	
    52	        page_started_at = time.monotonic()
    53	
    54	        response = requests.get(
    55	            url,
    56	            headers=headers,
    57	            params=params if page_count == 0 else None,
    58	            timeout=30,
    59	        )
    60	
    61	        request_elapsed = (
    62	            time.monotonic() - page_started_at
    63	        )
    64	
    65	        if progress_callback:
    66	            progress_callback(
    67	                f"Received HTTP {response.status_code} "
    68	                f"for page {next_page_number:,} "
    69	                f"after {request_elapsed:.1f}s"
    70	            )
    71	
    72	        response.raise_for_status()
    73	
    74	        response_data = response.json()
    75	        page_properties = (
    76	            response_data.get("value", []) or []
    77	        )
    78	
    79	        all_properties.extend(page_properties)
    80	        page_count += 1
    81	
    82	        next_url = response_data.get("@odata.nextLink")
    83	
    84	        if progress_callback:
    85	            progress_callback(
    86	                f"Completed DDF page {page_count:,}: "
    87	                f"{len(page_properties):,} listings | "
    88	                f"{len(all_properties):,} total | "
    89	                f"more pages: "
    90	                f"{'yes' if next_url else 'no'}"
    91	            )
    92	
    93	        url = next_url
    94	        params = None
    95	
    96	        if url:
    97	            time.sleep(0.2)
    98	
    99	    if (
   100	        progress_callback
   101	        and page_limit
   102	        and page_count >= page_limit
   103	        and url
   104	    ):
   105	        progress_callback(
   106	            f"Stopped after reaching "
   107	            f"--max-pages={page_limit}."
   108	        )
   109	
   110	    return all_properties, page_count

FILE: backend/mls/management/commands/sync_ddf_properties.py
================================================================
     1	
     2	import time
     3	from django.core.management.base import BaseCommand
     4	from django.db import transaction
     5	from mls.helpers import get_access_token
     6	from datetime import timedelta
     7	from mls.models import Property, Room, Media  # Replace with your actual app name
     8	from mls.services.map_aggregates import rebuild_h3_aggregates
     9	from mls.snapshot_utils import bulk_record_listing_first_seen
    10	from mls.services.ddf.converters import (
    11	    safe_bool,
    12	    safe_decimal,
    13	    safe_int,
    14	    safe_str,
    15	)
    16	from mls.services.ddf.mapper import map_property_defaults
    17	from mls.services.ddf.client import fetch_all_properties
    18	
    19	
    20	class Command(BaseCommand):
    21	    help = 'Ultra-fast full sync of REALTOR.ca DDF properties'
    22	
    23	    def add_arguments(self, parser):
    24	        parser.add_argument('--full', action='store_true', help='Force full sync (ignore incremental)')
    25	        parser.add_argument('--threads', type=int, default=10, help='Deprecated. Kept temporarily for compatibility. Use default threading.'
    26	        "DDF pagination is sequential")
    27	        parser.add_argument('--batch-size', type=int, default=5000, help='Properties per DB batch')
    28	        parser.add_argument(
    29	            '--max-pages',
    30	            type=int,
    31	            default=0,
    32	            help='Optional safety cap for pages during testing. 0 means no cap.',
    33	        )
    34	
    35	    def build_incremental_filter(self, force_full=False):
    36	        """
    37	        Build the DDF filter used for an incremental sync.
    38	
    39	        A full sync returns None, meaning no timestamp filter.
    40	        """
    41	        if force_full:
    42	            return None
    43	
    44	        latest_property = Property.objects.order_by(
    45	            "-modification_timestamp"
    46	        ).first()
    47	
    48	        if not latest_property:
    49	            return None
    50	
    51	        if not latest_property.modification_timestamp:
    52	            return None
    53	
    54	        cutoff = (
    55	            latest_property.modification_timestamp
    56	            - timedelta(minutes=10)
    57	        )
    58	
    59	        # return (
    60	        #     "ModificationTimestamp gt "
    61	        #     f"{cutoff.isoformat()}Z"
    62	        # )
    63	
    64	    def handle(self, *args, **options):
    65	        start_time = time.time()
    66	
    67	        token = get_access_token()
    68	
    69	        if not token:
    70	            self.stderr.write(
    71	                "Failed to get access token"
    72	            )
    73	            return
    74	
    75	        headers = {
    76	            "Authorization": f"Bearer {token}",
    77	        }
    78	
    79	        filter_expression = self.build_incremental_filter(
    80	            force_full=options["full"],
    81	        )
    82	
    83	        self.stdout.write(
    84	            "Downloading DDF properties..."
    85	        )
    86	
    87	        all_properties, page_count = fetch_all_properties(
    88	            headers=headers,
    89	            filter_expression=filter_expression,
    90	            max_pages=options["max_pages"],
    91	            progress_callback=self.stdout.write,
    92	        )
    93	
    94	        self.stdout.write(
    95	            f"Downloaded {page_count} pages containing "
    96	            f"{len(all_properties):,} listings."
    97	        )
    98	
    99	        if not all_properties:
   100	            self.stdout.write(
   101	                "No properties returned."
   102	            )
   103	            return
   104	
   105	        processed_keys = {
   106	            property_data.get("ListingKey")
   107	            for property_data in all_properties
   108	            if property_data.get("ListingKey")
   109	        }
   110	
   111	        self.stdout.write(
   112	            f"Starting bulk upsert of "
   113	            f"{len(all_properties):,} properties..."
   114	        )
   115	
   116	        self.bulk_upsert(
   117	            all_properties,
   118	            batch_size=options["batch_size"],
   119	        )
   120	
   121	
   122	        if options["full"]:
   123	            self.stdout.write(
   124	                "Full sync completed; checking for orphaned properties..."
   125	            )
   126	            self.cleanup_orphaned_properties(processed_keys)
   127	        else:
   128	            self.stdout.write(
   129	                "Incremental sync: skipping orphan cleanup."
   130	            )
   131	
   132	        self.stdout.write("Rebuilding H3 map aggregates...")
   133	        aggregate_cells = rebuild_h3_aggregates()
   134	        self.stdout.write(
   135	            self.style.SUCCESS(f"Built {aggregate_cells:,} aggregate cells")
   136	        )
   137	
   138	        elapsed = time.time() - start_time
   139	        self.stdout.write(self.style.SUCCESS(f"COMPLETED in {elapsed:.1f} seconds ({len(all_properties)/elapsed:.1f} props/sec)"))
   140	
   141	    def cleanup_orphaned_properties(self, processed_keys):
   142	        """Deletes properties tagged as DDF that were NOT seen in this sync."""
   143	        if not processed_keys:
   144	            return
   145	
   146	        # Safety Check: Don't delete if we processed suspiciously few properties
   147	        current_ddf_count = Property.objects.filter(category_type=Property.DDF).count()
   148	        if len(processed_keys) < (current_ddf_count * 0.5) and current_ddf_count > 100:
   149	            self.stdout.write(self.style.ERROR(
   150	                f"ABORTING CLEANUP: Processed {len(processed_keys)} listings, which is < 50% of "
   151	                f"current database count ({current_ddf_count}). This might indicate an API failure."
   152	            ))
   153	            return
   154	
   155	        self.stdout.write(f"Cleaning up orphaned MLS properties...")
   156	        orphans = Property.objects.filter(category_type=Property.DDF).exclude(listing_key__in=processed_keys)
   157	        orphan_count = orphans.count()
   158	        
   159	        if orphan_count > 0:
   160	            # Delete related rooms and media first (though Django usually handles CASCADE)
   161	            # Property.objects.filter(...) delete() handles cascade automatically if models are set up correctly.
   162	            orphans.delete()
   163	            self.stdout.write(self.style.SUCCESS(f"Deleted {orphan_count} orphaned MLS listings."))
   164	        else:
   165	            self.stdout.write("No orphaned listings found.")
   166	
   167	
   168	    @transaction.atomic
   169	    def bulk_upsert(self, properties_data, batch_size=5000):
   170	        # We'll process in batches to avoid memory explosion
   171	        for i in range(0, len(properties_data), batch_size):
   172	            batch = properties_data[i:i + batch_size]
   173	            self.process_batch(batch)
   174	            self.stdout.write(f"Processed batch {i//batch_size + 1}/{(len(properties_data)-1)//batch_size + 1}")
   175	
   176	    def process_batch(self, batch):
   177	        listing_keys = [p["ListingKey"] for p in batch if p.get("ListingKey")]
   178	        existing = Property.objects.filter(listing_key__in=listing_keys).in_bulk(field_name="listing_key")
   179	        existing_keys = set(existing.keys())
   180	
   181	        property_objs = []
   182	        room_objs = []
   183	        media_objs = []
   184	        properties_to_update = []
   185	        first_seen_rows = []
   186	
   187	        for data in batch:
   188	            key = data.get("ListingKey")
   189	            print(key)
   190	            if not key:
   191	                continue
   192	
   193	            defaults = map_property_defaults(data)
   194	           
   195	            first_seen_rows.append(
   196	                (key, defaults.get("modification_timestamp") or defaults.get("original_entry_timestamp"))
   197	            )
   198	
   199	            if key in existing:
   200	                prop = existing[key]
   201	                for field, value in defaults.items():
   202	                    setattr(prop, field, value)
   203	                properties_to_update.append(prop)
   204	            else:
   205	                prop = Property(listing_key=key, **defaults)
   206	                property_objs.append(prop)
   207	
   208	            # === Rooms ===
   209	            for r in data.get("Rooms", []):
   210	                room_objs.append(Room(
   211	                    property=prop,
   212	                    room_type=safe_str(r.get("RoomType")),
   213	                    room_length=safe_decimal(r.get("RoomLength")),
   214	                    room_width=safe_decimal(r.get("RoomWidth")),
   215	                    room_level=safe_str(r.get("RoomLevel")),
   216	                    room_description=safe_str(r.get("RoomDescription")),
   217	                    room_dimensions=safe_str(r.get("RoomDimensions")),
   218	                    room_length_width_units=safe_str(r.get("RoomLengthWidthUnits")),
   219	                ))
   220	
   221	            # === Media ===
   222	            for m in data.get("Media", []):
   223	                media_objs.append(Media(
   224	                    property=prop,
   225	                    media_url=safe_str(m.get("MediaURL")),
   226	                    media_category=safe_str(m.get("MediaCategory")),
   227	                    is_preferred=safe_bool(m.get("PreferredPhotoYN")),
   228	                    order=safe_int(m.get("Order"), 999),
   229	                ))
   230	
   231	        # === Final DB Operations ===
   232	        if property_objs:
   233	            Property.objects.bulk_create(property_objs, ignore_conflicts=False)
   234	
   235	        if properties_to_update:
   236	            Property.objects.bulk_update(
   237	                properties_to_update,
   238	                fields=[f.name for f in Property._meta.fields if f.name != "id" and f.name != "listing_key"]
   239	            )
   240	
   241	        # Replace rooms & media (faster than upsert)
   242	        if property_objs or properties_to_update:
   243	            affected_prop_ids = [p.id for p in (property_objs + properties_to_update) if hasattr(p, 'id')]
   244	            if affected_prop_ids:
   245	                Room.objects.filter(property_id__in=affected_prop_ids).delete()
   246	                Media.objects.filter(property_id__in=affected_prop_ids).delete()
   247	
   248	                if room_objs:
   249	                    Room.objects.bulk_create(room_objs, ignore_conflicts=True)
   250	                if media_objs:
   251	                    Media.objects.bulk_create(media_objs, ignore_conflicts=True)
   252	
   253	        if first_seen_rows:
   254	            bulk_record_listing_first_seen(first_seen_rows)
   255	
   256	
   257	# Incremental sync
   258	# python manage.py sync_ddf_properties --batch-size 8000
   259	
   260	# Full sync
   261	# python manage.py sync_ddf_properties --full --batch-size 8000

    20	// A preprocessor to extract the arrays from various forms
    21	const mediaPreprocessor = (val: any) => {
    22	  if (Array.isArray(val)) {
    23	    return val.map((m: any) => ({
    24	      media_url: m.media_url || m.MediaURL || "",
    25	      media_category: m.media_category || m.MediaCategory || "Property Photo",
    26	      is_preferred:
    27	        m.is_preferred !== undefined
    28	          ? m.is_preferred
    29	          : m.PreferredPhotoYN !== undefined
    30	            ? m.PreferredPhotoYN
    31	            : true,
    32	      order: m.order || m.Order || 0,
    33	    }));
    34	  }
    35	  if (typeof val === "object" && val && (val.media_url || val.MediaURL)) {
    36	    return [
    37	      {
    38	        media_url: val.media_url || val.MediaURL,
    39	        media_category:
    40	          val.media_category || val.MediaCategory || "Property Photo",
    41	        is_preferred: true,
    42	        order: 0,
    43	      },
    44	    ];
    45	  }
    46	  return [];
    47	};

   166	    const addressParts = [];
   167	    if (prop.unit_number) addressParts.push(`${prop.unit_number}-`);
   168	    if (prop.street_number) addressParts.push(prop.street_number);
   169	    if (prop.street_dir_prefix) addressParts.push(prop.street_dir_prefix);
   170	    if (prop.street_name) addressParts.push(prop.street_name);
   171	    if (prop.street_suffix) addressParts.push(prop.street_suffix);
   172	    if (prop.street_dir_suffix) addressParts.push(prop.street_dir_suffix);
   173	    const builtAddress = addressParts.join(" ").trim();

   175	    // 2. Identify Keys
   176	    const bestKey =
   177	      prop.listing_key ||
   178	      prop.listingKey ||
   179	      prop.ListingKey ||
   180	      prop.PropertyKey ||
   181	      prop.id ||
   182	      "";
   183	
   184	    // 3. Resolve Fallbacks
   185	    const resolvedMedia = prop.media || prop.Media || [];
   186	    if (prop.Photos && resolvedMedia.length === 0) {
   187	      prop.Photos.forEach((p: any) => {
   188	        resolvedMedia.push({
   189	          media_url: p.PhotoURL || p,
   190	          media_category: "Property Photo",
   191	          is_preferred: true,
   192	          order: 0,
   193	        });
   194	      });
   195	    }
   196	
   197	    const priceRaw = prop.list_price ?? prop.ListPrice;
   198	    const resolvedPrice =
   199	      typeof priceRaw === "string" ? parseFloat(priceRaw) : priceRaw || 0;
   200	
   201	    const resolvedCity = prop.city || prop.City || "";
   202	    const resolvedProvince =
   203	      prop.state_or_province || prop.StateOrProvince || "ON";
   204	    const resolvedSubType =
   205	      prop.property_sub_type ||
   206	      prop.PropertySubType ||
   207	      prop.PropertyType ||
   208	      "Property";
   209	    const resolvedBedrooms = parseInt(
   210	      String(prop.bedrooms_total || prop.BedroomsTotal || 0),
   211	    );
   212	    const resolvedBathrooms = parseInt(
   213	      String(prop.bathrooms_total_integer || prop.BathroomsTotalInteger || 0),
   214	    );
   215	    const resolvedStatus =
   216	      prop.standard_status || prop.StandardStatus || "Active";
   217	    const resolvedAddress =
   218	      prop.unparsed_address || builtAddress || prop.address || "";
   219	    const resolvedPostal = prop.postal_code || prop.PostalCode || "";
   220	
   221	    // 4. Create Standardized Object
   222	    return {
   223	      ...prop, // Retain source fields, then override with canonical normalized fields.
   224	      PropertyKey: bestKey,
   225	      ListingKey: bestKey,
   226	      list_price: prop.list_price,
   227	      listing_key: bestKey,
   228	      ListPrice: resolvedPrice,
   229	      City: resolvedCity,
   230	      city: prop.city,
   231	      StateOrProvince: resolvedProvince,
   232	      PropertySubType: resolvedSubType,
   233	      BedroomsTotal: resolvedBedrooms,
   234	      bedrooms_total: prop.bedrooms_total,
   235	      BathroomsTotalInteger: resolvedBathrooms,
   236	      bathrooms_total_integer: prop.bathrooms_total_integer,
   237	      StandardStatus: resolvedStatus,
   238	      standard_status: prop.standard_status,
   239	      ModificationTimestamp:
   240	        prop.ModificationTimestamp || new Date().toISOString(),
   241	      unparsed_address: prop.unparsed_address,
   242	      postal_code: prop.postal_code,
   243	      latitude: prop.latitude ?? prop.Latitude,
   244	      longitude: prop.longitude ?? prop.Longitude,
   245	      public_remarks: prop.public_remarks || prop.PublicRemarks,
   246	      media: resolvedMedia,
   247	      rooms: prop.rooms || prop.Rooms || [],
   248	      category_type: prop.category_type,
   249	      photos_count: prop.photos_count,
   250	      listing_url: prop.listing_url,
   251	      building_area_total:
   252	        prop.building_area_total || prop.LivingArea || prop.LivingAreaMinimum,
   253	      year_built: prop.year_built || prop.YearBuilt,
   254	
   255	      // UI Support Fields
   256	      address: resolvedAddress,
   257	      location: resolvedCity,
   258	      province: resolvedProvince,
   259	      postalCode: resolvedPostal,
   260	      cooling: (() => {
   261	        const v = prop.cooling || prop.Cooling;
   262	        return Array.isArray(v) ? v.join(", ") : v || "";
   263	      })(),
   264	      basement: (() => {
   265	        const v = prop.basement || prop.Basement;
   266	        return Array.isArray(v) ? v.join(", ") : v || "";
   267	      })(),
   268	      zoning: prop.zoning || prop.Zoning || "",
   269	      parking_total: prop.parking_total || prop.ParkingTotal || 0,
   270	      parking_features: (() => {
   271	        const v = prop.parking_features || prop.ParkingFeatures;
   272	        return Array.isArray(v) ? v.join(", ") : v || "";
   273	      })(),
   274	      total_actual_rent:
   275	        prop.total_actual_rent == null ? "" : String(prop.total_actual_rent),
   276	
   277	      // Legacy Support
   278	      Photos: resolvedMedia.map((m: any) => ({ PhotoURL: m.media_url })),
   279	      Media: resolvedMedia,
   280	      Rooms: prop.rooms || prop.Rooms || [],
   281	      LivingArea:
   282	        prop.building_area_total || prop.LivingArea || prop.LivingAreaMinimum
   283	          ? parseFloat(
   284	              String(
   285	                prop.building_area_total ||
   286	                  prop.LivingArea ||
   287	                  prop.LivingAreaMinimum,
   288	              ),
   289	            )
   290	          : null,
   291	      YearBuilt:
   292	        prop.year_built || prop.YearBuilt
   293	          ? parseInt(String(prop.year_built || prop.YearBuilt))
   294	          : null,
   295	      PublicRemarks: prop.public_remarks || prop.PublicRemarks,
   296	      PostalCode: resolvedPostal,
   297	      Latitude: prop.latitude,
   298	      Longitude: prop.longitude,
   299	      Description: prop.public_remarks || prop.PublicRemarks,
   300	      PropertyType: resolvedSubType,
   301	    };
   302	  });

    30	const CLIENT_CACHE_PREFIX = "mls:api-cache:";
    31	const CLIENT_CACHE_TTL_MS = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 24 hours
    32	const MAP_FILTER_CACHE_TTL_MS = 60 * 1000; // 60 seconds for interactive map requests
    33	const clientMemoryCache = new Map<
    34	  string,
    35	  { timestamp: number; data: unknown }
    36	>();
    37	const mapFilterMemoryCache = new Map<
    38	  string,
    39	  { timestamp: number; data: unknown }
    40	>();
    41	
    42	export interface ListingFallbackMeta {
    43	  fallback_applied?: boolean;
    44	  fallback_stage?: string | null;
    45	  suggested_locations?: string[];
    46	}

    59	function getClientCachedResponse<T>(cacheKey: string): T | null {
    60	  const now = Date.now();
    61	  const inMemory = clientMemoryCache.get(cacheKey);
    62	  if (inMemory && now - inMemory.timestamp < CLIENT_CACHE_TTL_MS) {
    63	    return inMemory.data as T;
    64	  }
    65	
    66	  if (typeof window === "undefined") return null;
    67	
    68	  try {
    69	    const raw = window.localStorage.getItem(
    70	      `${CLIENT_CACHE_PREFIX}${cacheKey}`,
    71	    );
    72	    if (!raw) return null;
    73	
    74	    const parsed = JSON.parse(raw) as { timestamp?: number; data?: T };
    75	    if (
    76	      !parsed ||
    77	      typeof parsed.timestamp !== "number" ||
    78	      now - parsed.timestamp >= CLIENT_CACHE_TTL_MS
    79	    ) {
    80	      window.localStorage.removeItem(`${CLIENT_CACHE_PREFIX}${cacheKey}`);
    81	      return null;
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    clientMemoryCache.set(cacheKey, {
    85	      timestamp: parsed.timestamp,
    86	      data: parsed.data,
    87	    });
    88	
    89	    return (parsed.data ?? null) as T | null;
    90	  } catch {
    91	    return null;
    92	  }
    93	}
    94	
    95	function setClientCachedResponse<T>(cacheKey: string, data: T): void {
    96	  const entry = { timestamp: Date.now(), data };
    97	  clientMemoryCache.set(cacheKey, entry);
    98	
    99	  if (typeof window === "undefined") return;
   100	
   101	  try {
   102	    window.localStorage.setItem(
   103	      `${CLIENT_CACHE_PREFIX}${cacheKey}`,
   104	      JSON.stringify(entry),
   105	    );
   106	  } catch {
   107	    // Ignore storage quota / serialization errors and continue without persistence.
   108	  }
   109	}
   110	
   111	/**
   112	 * Maps static WP JSON Pre-Construction data to our standard Property schema
   113	 */
   114	export function mapPreconToProperty(p: any): Property {
   115	  const meta = p.property_meta || {};
   116	  const getMetaStr = (key: string) =>
   117	    meta[key] && meta[key][0] ? meta[key][0] : "";
   118	
   119	  const priceStr = getMetaStr("fave_property_price") || "0";
   120	  const bedrooms = getMetaStr("fave_property_bedrooms") || "0";
   121	  const bathrooms = getMetaStr("fave_property_bathrooms") || "0";
   122	  const sizeStr = getMetaStr("fave_property_size") || "";
   123	  const address =
   124	    getMetaStr("fave_property_address") || p.title?.rendered || "";
   125	  const developer = getMetaStr("fave_developer") || "";
   126	  const completion = getMetaStr("fave_estimated-completion") || "";
   127	  const mainImage = p.yoast_head_json?.og_image?.[0]?.url || "";
   128	  const projectName = p.title?.rendered || "";
   129	
   130	  return normalizeListingRecord({
   131	    listing_key: `precon_${p.id}`,
   132	    listing_id: `precon_${p.id}`,
   133	    ListingKey: `precon_${p.id}`,
   134	    PropertyKey: `precon_${p.id}`,
   135	    address: address.trim(),
   136	    city: "Pre-Construction",
   137	    City: "Pre-Construction",
   138	    list_price: priceStr,
   139	    ListPrice: parseFloat(priceStr) || 0,
   140	    bedrooms_total: bedrooms,
   141	    bathrooms_total_integer: bathrooms,
   142	    building_area_total: sizeStr,
   143	    standard_status: "Pre-Construction",
   144	    StandardStatus: "Pre-Construction",
   145	    developer,
   146	    estimated_completion: completion,
   147	    property_sub_type: "Pre-Construction",
   148	    PropertySubType: "Pre-Construction",
   149	    public_remarks: p.content?.rendered?.replace(/<[^>]*>?/gm, "").trim(),
   150	    PublicRemarks: p.content?.rendered?.replace(/<[^>]*>?/gm, "").trim(),
   151	    media: [{ media_url: mainImage, is_preferred: true, order: 1 } as any],
   152	    project_name: projectName,
   153	  });
   154	}
   155	
   156	/**
   157	 * Helper function to map API response to Property interface
   158	 */
   159	export function mapPropertyFromAPI(prop: any): Property {
   160	  const normalized = normalizeListingRecord(prop);
   161	  try {
   162	    return PropertyResponseSchema.parse(normalized) as Property;
   163	  } catch (error) {
   164	    console.error(
   165	      "Zod Schema Parsing Error for property:",
   166	      normalized?.id || normalized?.listing_key,
   167	      error,
   168	    );
   169	    // Fallback simply returns the messy object if parsing critically fails
   170	    return normalized as Property;
   171	  }
   172	}
   173	
   174	// The mapEstatePropertyFromAPI function is specifically designed to handle the unique structure of estate properties, which may differ from our standard property schema. It first normalizes the raw estate data and then maps it to our Property interface, ensuring that we can work with estate listings seamlessly alongside regular MLS properties.
   175	
   176	export function mapEstatePropertyFromAPI(prop: any, id?: string): Property {
   177	  console.log(
   178	    "[estate-map] Debug: Raw data received in mapEstatePropertyFromAPI:",
   179	    prop,
   180	  );
   181	  const normalized = normalizeEstateDetailRecord(prop, id);
   182	  console.log("[estate-map] Debug: Data after normalization:", normalized);
   183	  const finalProperty = mapPropertyFromAPI(normalized);
   184	  console.log("[estate-map] Debug: Final property object:", finalProperty);
   185	  return finalProperty;
   186	}
   187	
   188	/**
   189	 * Search properties by query string (city, address, postal code, keywords)
   190	 */
   191	export async function searchProperties(
   192	  query: string,
   193	  extraFilters?: Record<string, any>,
   194	): Promise<Property[]> {
   195	  try {
   196	    const params: Record<string, any> = { search: query, ...extraFilters };
   197	    const data = (await fetchFilteredProperties(params)) as any;
   198	    const results: any[] = data.results || data.value || [];
   199	    return results.map(mapPropertyFromAPI);
   200	  } catch (error) {
   201	    console.error("Error searching properties:", error);
   202	    return [];
   203	  }
   204	}
   205	
   206	/**
   207	 * Fetch properties with basic filters
   208	 */
   209	export async function fetchProperties(
   210	  filters?: PropertyFilterParams,
   211	): Promise<Property[]> {
   212	  try {
   213	    const exclusiveFilters: ExclusivePropertyFilterParams = {};
   214	
   215	    if (filters) {
   216	      if (filters.province) {
   217	        const provinceMapping: { [key: string]: string } = {
   218	          Ontario: "ON",
   219	          Quebec: "QC",
   220	          "British Columbia": "BC",
   221	          Alberta: "AB",
   222	          Manitoba: "MB",
   223	          Saskatchewan: "SK",
   224	          "Nova Scotia": "NS",
   225	          "New Brunswick": "NB",
   226	          "Newfoundland and Labrador": "NL",
   227	          "Prince Edward Island": "PE",
   228	          "Northwest Territories": "NT",
   229	          Nunavut: "NU",
   230	          Yukon: "YT",
   231	        };
   232	        exclusiveFilters.province =
   233	          provinceMapping[filters.province] || filters.province;
   234	      }
   235	
   236	      if (filters.city) exclusiveFilters.city = filters.city;
   237	      if (filters.price_min) exclusiveFilters.price_min = filters.price_min;
   238	      if (filters.price_max) exclusiveFilters.price_max = filters.price_max;
   239	      if (filters.bedrooms) exclusiveFilters.bedrooms = filters.bedrooms;
   240	      if (filters.bathrooms) exclusiveFilters.bathrooms = filters.bathrooms;
   241	
   242	      if (filters.property_subtype) {
   243	        exclusiveFilters.property_sub_type = filters.property_subtype;
   244	      }
   245	
   246	      if (filters.status) {
   247	        exclusiveFilters.standard_status = filters.status;
   248	      }
   249	    }
   250	
   251	    const response = await fetchExclusiveProperties(exclusiveFilters);
   252	
   253	    return (response.results || []).map((prop: any) =>
   254	      mapPropertyFromAPI(prop),
   255	    );
   256	  } catch (error) {
   257	    console.error("Error fetching properties:", error);
   258	    return [];
   259	  }
   260	}
   261	
   262	/**
   263	 * Fetch exclusive properties with detailed filters
   264	 */
   265	export async function fetchExclusiveProperties(
   266	  filters?: ExclusivePropertyFilterParams,
   267	): Promise<ExclusivePropertiesResponse> {
   268	  try {
   269	    const queryParams = new URLSearchParams();
   270	
   271	    const limit = filters?.limit || 12;
   272	    const offset = filters?.offset || 0;
   273	
   274	    queryParams.append("limit", limit.toString());
   275	    queryParams.append("offset", offset.toString());
   276	
   277	    if (filters) {
   278	      Object.entries(filters).forEach(([key, value]) => {
   279	        if (key === "limit" || key === "offset") return;
   280	
   281	        if (value !== undefined && value !== null && value !== "") {
   282	          const queryKey = key === "property_sub_type" ? "property_type" : key;
   283	          if (typeof value === "boolean") {
   284	            queryParams.append(queryKey, value ? "true" : "false");
   285	          } else {
   286	            queryParams.append(queryKey, value.toString());
   287	          }
   288	        }
   289	      });
   290	    }
   291	
   292	    const url = `${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/properties/exclusive-properties/${queryParams.toString() ? "?" + queryParams.toString() : ""}`;
   293	    const cacheKey = `exclusive:${queryParams.toString()}`;
   294	    const cached =
   295	      getClientCachedResponse<ExclusivePropertiesResponse>(cacheKey);
   296	    if (cached) return cached;
   297	
   298	    const response = await fetchAPI<ExclusivePropertiesResponse>(url, {
   299	      cache: "no-store",
   300	    });
   301	    const normalizedResponse: ExclusivePropertiesResponse = {
   302	      ...response,
   303	      results: (response.results || []).map((row) => mapPropertyFromAPI(row)),
   304	    };
   305	    setClientCachedResponse(cacheKey, normalizedResponse);
   306	    return normalizedResponse;
   307	  } catch (error) {
   308	    console.error("Error fetching exclusive properties:", error);
   309	    return {
   310	      results: [],
   311	      count: 0,
   312	      next: null,
   313	      previous: null,
   314	      updated_to_exclusive: 0,
   315	      fallback_applied: false,
   316	      fallback_stage: null,
   317	      suggested_locations: [],
   318	    };
   319	  }
   320	}
   321	
   322	/**
   323	 * Fetch lease properties with detailed filters
   324	 */
   325	export async function fetchLeaseProperties(
   326	  filters?: LeasePropertyFilterParams,
   327	): Promise<{
   328	  results: any[];
   329	  count: number;
   330	  next: number | null;
   331	  previous: number | null;
   332	}> {
   333	  try {
   334	    const queryParams = new URLSearchParams();
   335	
   336	    const limit = filters?.limit || 6;
   337	    const offset = filters?.offset || 0;
   338	
   339	    queryParams.append("limit", limit.toString());
   340	    queryParams.append("offset", offset.toString());
   341	
   342	    if (filters) {
   343	      Object.entries(filters).forEach(([key, value]) => {
   344	        if (key === "limit" || key === "offset") return;
   345	
   346	        if (value !== undefined && value !== null && value !== "") {
   347	          const queryKey = key === "property_sub_type" ? "property_type" : key;
   348	          if (typeof value === "boolean") {
   349	            queryParams.append(queryKey, value ? "true" : "false");
   350	          } else {
   351	            queryParams.append(queryKey, value.toString());
   352	          }
   353	        }
   354	      });
   355	    }
   356	
   357	    const url = `${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/properties/lease-properties/${queryParams.toString() ? "?" + queryParams.toString() : ""}`;
   358	    const cacheKey = `lease:${queryParams.toString()}`;
   359	    const cached = getClientCachedResponse<{
   360	      results: any[];
   361	      count: number;
   362	      next: number | null;
   363	      previous: number | null;
   364	    }>(cacheKey);
   365	    if (cached) return cached;
   366	
   367	    const response = await fetchAPI<{
   368	      results: any[];
   369	      count: number;
   370	      next: number | null;
   371	      previous: number | null;
   372	    }>(url, { cache: "no-store" });
   373	    const normalizedResponse = {
   374	      ...response,
   375	      results: (response.results || []).map((row) => mapPropertyFromAPI(row)),
   376	    };
   377	    setClientCachedResponse(cacheKey, normalizedResponse);
   378	    return normalizedResponse;
   379	  } catch (error) {
   380	    console.error("Error fetching lease properties:", error);
   381	    return {
   382	      results: [],
   383	      count: 0,
   384	      next: null,
   385	      previous: null,
   386	    };
   387	  }
   388	}
   389	
   390	/**
   391	 * Generic filtered properties fetcher
   392	 */
   393	export async function fetchFilteredProperties(
   394	  filters: Record<string, any>,
   395	  requestOptions?: RequestInit,
   396	): Promise<any> {
   397	  const params = buildFilterSearchParams(filters);
   398	
   399	  const url = `${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/properties/filter/?${params.toString()}`;
   400	  const hasMapBounds =
   401	    params.has("lat_min") &&
   402	    params.has("lat_max") &&
   403	    params.has("lng_min") &&
   404	    params.has("lng_max");
   405	  const mapCacheKey = `map-filter:${params.toString()}`;
   406	  if (hasMapBounds) {
   407	    const cached = mapFilterMemoryCache.get(mapCacheKey);
   408	    if (cached && Date.now() - cached.timestamp < MAP_FILTER_CACHE_TTL_MS) {
   409	      return cached.data;
   410	    }
   411	  }
   412	  // console.log("FILTER URL →", url);
   413	
   414	  try {
   415	    const response = await fetchAPI<any>(url, {
   416	      cache: "no-store",
   417	      ...requestOptions,
   418	    });
   419	    const normalizedResponse =
   420	      response && Array.isArray(response.results)
   421	        ? { ...response, results: response.results.map(mapPropertyFromAPI) }
   422	        : response;
   423	    if (hasMapBounds) {
   424	      mapFilterMemoryCache.set(mapCacheKey, {
   425	        timestamp: Date.now(),
   426	        data: normalizedResponse,
   427	      });
   428	    }
   429	    return normalizedResponse;
   430	  } catch (error) {
   431	    console.error("Filter API error:", error);
   432	    return { results: [], count: 0 };
   433	  }
   434	}

   436	const DEFAULT_PROPERTY_TYPES: PropertyTypeOption[] = [
   437	  { value: "Detached", label: "Detached" },
   438	  { value: "Semi-Detached", label: "Semi-Detached" },
   439	  { value: "Condo Apt", label: "Condo Apt" },
   440	  { value: "Freehold Townhouse", label: "Freehold Townhouse" },
   441	  { value: "Condo Townhouse", label: "Condo Townhouse" },
   442	];

   444	/**
   445	 * Fetch available property types for filters.
   446	 */
   447	export async function fetchPropertyTypes(params?: {
   448	  province?: string;
   449	  listing_type?: "all" | "exclusive" | "lease" | "precon" | "community";
   450	}): Promise<PropertyTypeOption[]> {
   451	  try {
   452	    const query = new URLSearchParams();
   453	    if (params?.province) query.append("province", params.province);
   454	    if (params?.listing_type) query.append("listing_type", params.listing_type);
   455	
   456	    const url = `${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/properties/property-types/${query.toString() ? `?${query.toString()}` : ""}`;
   457	    const data = await fetchAPI<{ results?: PropertyTypeOption[] }>(url, {
   458	      cache: "no-store",
   459	    });
   460	    const results = Array.isArray(data?.results) ? data.results : [];
   461	
   462	    if (results.length === 0) return DEFAULT_PROPERTY_TYPES;
   463	
   464	    return results.filter(
   465	      (item) =>
   466	        !!item && typeof item.value === "string" && item.value.trim() !== "",
   467	    );
   468	  } catch (error) {
   469	    console.error("Error fetching property types:", error);
   470	    return DEFAULT_PROPERTY_TYPES;
   471	  }
   472	}

   474	export async function fetchHomepageCategoryCatalog(): Promise<HomepageCategoryCatalog> {
   475	  try {
   476	    const [
   477	      exclusiveResponse,
   478	      rentalResponse,
   479	      preconResponse,
   480	      communityResponse,
   481	      newlyListedResponse,
   482	      propertyTypes,
   483	    ] = await Promise.all([
   484	      fetchExclusiveProperties({ limit: 1, offset: 0 }),
   485	      fetchLeaseProperties({ limit: 1, offset: 0 }),
   486	      fetchPreConnProperties({ limit: 1, offset: 0 }),
   487	      fetchCommunityProperties({ limit: 1, offset: 0 }),
   488	      fetchNewlyListedProperties({ limit: 1, offset: 0 }),
   489	      fetchPropertyTypes({ listing_type: "exclusive" }),
   490	    ]);
   491	
   492	    const baseCategories: HomepageCategory[] = [
   493	      {
   494	        key: "newly_listed",
   495	        kind: "newly_listed",
   496	        label: "Newly Listed Properties",
   497	        count: newlyListedResponse.count || 0,
   498	        enabled: true,
   499	        route: "/new-listings",
   500	        source: "backend",
   501	        order: 10,
   502	      },
   503	      {
   504	        key: "exclusive",
   505	        kind: "exclusive",
   506	        label: "Exclusive Properties",
   507	        count: exclusiveResponse.count || 0,
   508	        enabled: true,
   509	        route: "/listing",
   510	        source: "backend",
   511	        order: 20,
   512	      },
   513	      {
   514	        key: "community",
   515	        kind: "community",
   516	        label: "Community Listings",
   517	        count: communityResponse.count || 0,
   518	        enabled: true,
   519	        route: "/community-listings",
   520	        source: "backend",
   521	        order: 25,
   522	      },
   523	      {
   524	        key: "rental",
   525	        kind: "rental",
   526	        label: "Rental Properties",
   527	        count: rentalResponse.count || 0,
   528	        enabled: true,
   529	        route: "/listing/rental",
   530	        source: "backend",
   531	        order: 30,
   532	      },
   533	      {
   534	        key: "precon",
   535	        kind: "precon",
   536	        label: "Pre-Construction Properties",
   537	        count: preconResponse.count || 0,
   538	        enabled: true,
   539	        route: "/pre-construction",
   540	        source: "backend",
   541	        order: 40,
   542	      },
   543	    ];
   544	
   545	    const typeCategories: HomepageCategory[] = propertyTypes.map((item) => ({
   546	      key: buildPropertyTypeCategoryKey(item.value),
   547	      kind: "property_type",
   548	      label: item.label,
   549	      count: typeof item.count === "number" ? item.count : Number.NaN,
   550	      enabled: true,
   551	      route: "/listing",
   552	      query: { property_type: item.value },
   553	      source: "backend",
   554	      order: 100,
   555	    }));
   556	
   557	    const categories = mergeHomepageCategories([
   558	      ...baseCategories,
   559	      ...typeCategories,
   560	    ]);
   561	    return {
   562	      categories,
   563	      fetchedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
   564	    };
   565	  } catch (error) {
   566	    console.error("Error fetching homepage category catalog:", error);
   567	    return {
   568	      categories: mergeHomepageCategories([]),
   569	      fetchedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
   570	    };
   571	  }
   572	}

   604	/**
   605	 * Fetch a single property by its key
   606	 */
   607	export async function fetchPropertyByKey(
   608	  propertyKey: string,
   609	): Promise<Property | null> {
   610	  try {
   611	    if (
   612	      propertyKey.startsWith("precon_") ||
   613	      propertyKey.startsWith("property-")
   614	    ) {
   615	      if (propertyKey.startsWith("precon_")) {
   616	        const idStr = propertyKey.replace("precon_", "");
   617	        return await fetchWPPreconPropertyAction(idStr);
   618	      }
   619	      // Synthetic key from CompareContext, just return null
   620	      return null;
   621	    }
   622	
   623	    if (propertyKey.startsWith("estate_")) {
   624	      const idStr = propertyKey.replace("estate_", "");
   625	      const estateData = await fetchAPI<any>(
   626	        `${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/estate-properties/${encodeURIComponent(idStr)}/`,
   627	        { cache: "no-store" },
   628	      );
   629	      return mapEstatePropertyFromAPI(estateData, idStr);
   630	    }
   631	
   632	    // console.log("Fetching property by key:", propertyKey);
   633	    let data: any;
   634	    try {
   635	      data = await fetchAPI<any>(
   636	        `${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/properties/${propertyKey}/`,
   637	        {
   638	          next: { revalidate: 300 }, // Cache for 5 minutes
   639	        },
   640	      );
   641	    } catch (mlsError: any) {
   642	      const mlsErrorMsg = String(mlsError?.message || "");
   643	      const isInvalidPrimaryKey =
   644	        mlsErrorMsg.includes("API_ERROR:400") &&
   645	        mlsErrorMsg.toLowerCase().includes("primary key is invalid");
   646	
   647	      // Fallback: key may be estate listing_key (e.g. EST-2026-0001) not prefixed in URL.
   648	      if (isInvalidPrimaryKey) {
   649	        const estateList = await fetchAPI<any>(
   650	          `${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/estate-properties/?search=${encodeURIComponent(propertyKey)}&page_size=5`,
   651	          { cache: "no-store" },
   652	        );
   653	        const exact =
   654	          (estateList?.results || []).find(
   655	            (r: any) => r?.listing_key === propertyKey,
   656	          ) || (estateList?.results || [])[0];
   657	        if (exact) {
   658	          return mapEstatePropertyFromAPI(exact, String(exact?.id || ""));
   659	        }
   660	      }
   661	      throw mlsError;
   662	    }
   663	    return {
   664	      ...mapPropertyFromAPI(data),
   665	      PropertyKey: data.listing_key || propertyKey,
   666	      ListingKey: data.listing_key || propertyKey,
   667	    };
   668	  } catch (error: any) {
   669	    const errorMsg = error.message || "";
   670	    // Check if it's a "Not Found" error (either status 404 or OData 404 wrapped in 400)
   671	    if (
   672	      errorMsg.includes(":404:") ||
   673	      errorMsg.includes("not exist") ||
   674	      errorMsg.includes("does not exist")
   675	    ) {
   676	      console.warn(
   677	        `Property with key ${propertyKey} not found or no longer available.`,
   678	      );
   679	      return null;
   680	    }
   681	
   682	    console.error(`Unexpected error fetching property ${propertyKey}:`, error);
   683	    return null;
   684	  }
   685	}
   686	
   687	export async function fetchEstatePropertyById(
   688	  estateIdOrKey: string,
   689	): Promise<Property | null> {
   690	  const raw = String(estateIdOrKey || "").trim();
   691	  if (!raw) {
   692	    console.log(
   693	      "[estate-fetch] Debug: estateIdOrKey is empty, returning null.",
   694	    );
   695	    return null;
   696	  }
   697	
   698	  const normalized = raw.replace(/^estate_/i, "");
   699	  const asNumericId = /^\d+$/.test(normalized) ? normalized : null;
   700	
   701	  console.log(
   702	    `[estate-fetch] Debug: Starting fetch for estate property. Raw key: "${raw}", Normalized: "${normalized}", Numeric ID: ${asNumericId}`,
   703	  );
   704	
   705	  const findBySearch = async (): Promise<Property | null> => {
   706	    const candidates = Array.from(
   707	      new Set([raw, normalized, `estate_${normalized}`].filter(Boolean)),
   708	    );
   709	    console.log("[estate-fetch] Debug: Search candidates:", candidates);
   710	
   711	    for (const candidate of candidates) {
   712	      if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production") {
   713	        console.info(
   714	          `[estate-fetch] search candidate=${candidate} url=${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/estate-properties/?search=${encodeURIComponent(candidate)}&page_size=10`,
   715	        );
   716	      }
   717	      try {
   718	        const estateList = await fetchAPI<any>(
   719	          `${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/estate-properties/?search=${encodeURIComponent(candidate)}&page_size=10`,
   720	          { cache: "no-store" },
   721	        );
   722	
   723	        console.log(
   724	          `[estate-fetch] Debug: API response for candidate "${candidate}":`,
   725	          estateList,
   726	        );
   727	
   728	        const rows = estateList?.results || [];
   729	        console.log(
   730	          `[estate-fetch] Debug: Found ${rows.length} rows for candidate "${candidate}".`,
   731	        );
   732	
   733	        const exact =
   734	          rows.find(
   735	            (r: any) =>
   736	              String(r?.listing_key || "").toLowerCase() ===
   737	                candidate.toLowerCase() ||
   738	              String(r?.listing_key || "").toLowerCase() ===
   739	                raw.toLowerCase() ||
   740	              String(r?.listing_key || "").toLowerCase() ===
   741	                `estate_${normalized}`.toLowerCase() ||
   742	              String(r?.id || "") === normalized,
   743	          ) || rows[0];
   744	
   745	        if (exact) {
   746	          console.log("[estate-fetch] Debug: Found an exact match.", exact);
   747	          return mapEstatePropertyFromAPI(
   748	            exact,
   749	            String(exact?.id || normalized),
   750	          );
   751	        }
   752	      } catch (error) {
   753	        console.error(
   754	          `[estate-fetch] Error fetching or processing candidate "${candidate}":`,
   755	          error,
   756	        );
   757	      }
   758	    }
   759	    console.log(
   760	      "[estate-fetch] Debug: No property found after trying all candidates.",
   761	    );
   762	    return null;
   763	  };
   764	
   765	  try {
   766	    if (asNumericId) {
   767	      try {
   768	        if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production") {
   769	          console.info(
   770	            `[estate-fetch] direct id=${asNumericId} url=${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/estate-properties/${encodeURIComponent(asNumericId)}/`,
   771	          );
   772	        }
   773	        const estateData = await fetchAPI<any>(
   774	          `${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/estate-properties/${encodeURIComponent(asNumericId)}/`,
   775	          { cache: "no-store" },
   776	        );
   777	        console.log(
   778	          `[estate-fetch] Debug: API response for direct ID fetch (id: ${asNumericId}):`,
   779	          estateData,
   780	        );
   781	        if (estateData && estateData.id) {
   782	          console.log(
   783	            `[estate-fetch] Debug: Found data for direct ID ${asNumericId}.`,
   784	          );
   785	          return mapEstatePropertyFromAPI(estateData, asNumericId);
   786	        }
   787	        console.log(
   788	          `[estate-fetch] Debug: No data or invalid data returned for direct ID ${asNumericId}.`,
   789	        );
   790	        // Fallback to search if direct fetch fails
   791	        return await findBySearch();
   792	      } catch (idError: any) {
   793	        const msg = String(idError?.message || "");
   794	        if (!msg.includes("API_ERROR:404")) {
   795	          console.error(
   796	            `[estate-fetch] Error fetching direct ID ${asNumericId}:`,
   797	            idError,
   798	          );
   799	          // Decide if you want to stop or fallback
   800	          // For now, we'll log the error and fallback to search
   801	        }
   802	        if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production") {
   803	          console.warn(
   804	            `[estate-fetch] direct 404 for id=${asNumericId} or other error; falling back to search`,
   805	          );
   806	        }
   807	      }
   808	    }
   809	
   810	    return await findBySearch();
   811	  } catch (error) {
   812	    console.error(
   813	      `Unexpected error fetching estate property ${estateIdOrKey}:`,
   814	      error,
   815	    );
   816	    return null;
   817	  }
   818	}

   824	  return fetchProperties({ province: "Ontario" });
   825	}
   826	
   827	/**
   828	 * Compare multiple properties
   829	 */
   830	export async function fetchCompareProperties(propertyKeys: string[]): Promise<{
   831	  results: Property[];
   832	  count: number;
   833	}> {
   834	  try {
   835	    if (propertyKeys.length === 0) {
   836	      return { results: [], count: 0 };
   837	    }
   838	
   839	    // Partition keys into pre-construction and MLS keys
   840	    const preConKeys = propertyKeys.filter((k) => k.startsWith("precon_"));
   841	    const estateKeys = propertyKeys.filter((k) => k.startsWith("estate_"));
   842	    const mlsKeys = propertyKeys.filter(
   843	      (k) =>
   844	        !k.startsWith("precon_") &&
   845	        !k.startsWith("estate_") &&
   846	        !k.startsWith("property-"),
   847	    );
   848	
   849	    // Fetch pre-con ones locally via new WP fetch
   850	    const preConResults = (
   851	      await Promise.all(
   852	        preConKeys.map(async (k) => {
   853	          const idStr = k.replace("precon_", "");
   854	          return await fetchWPPreconPropertyAction(idStr);
   855	        }),
   856	      )
   857	    ).filter(Boolean) as Property[];
   858	
   859	    const estateResults = (
   860	      await Promise.all(
   861	        estateKeys.map(async (k) => {
   862	          const idStr = k.replace("estate_", "");
   863	          try {
   864	            const data = await fetchAPI<any>(
   865	              `${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/estate-properties/${encodeURIComponent(idStr)}/`,
   866	              { cache: "no-store" },
   867	            );
   868	            return mapEstatePropertyFromAPI(data, idStr);
   869	          } catch {
   870	            return null;
   871	          }
   872	        }),
   873	      )
   874	    ).filter(Boolean) as Property[];
   875	
   876	    let mlsResults: Property[] = [];
   877	
   878	    if (mlsKeys.length > 0) {
   879	      const queryParams = new URLSearchParams();
   880	      mlsKeys.forEach((key) => {
   881	        if (key && key.trim()) {
   882	          queryParams.append("listing_key", key.trim());
   883	        }
   884	      });
   885	
   886	      const url = `${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/properties/compare/?${queryParams.toString()}`;
   887	
   888	      try {
   889	        const responseData = await fetchAPI<any>(url, { cache: "no-store" });
   890	
   891	        const resultsArray =
   892	          responseData.results ||
   893	          responseData.data ||
   894	          responseData.properties ||
   895	          responseData ||
   896	          [];
   897	
   898	        if (Array.isArray(resultsArray)) {
   899	          mlsResults = resultsArray.map((prop: any) =>
   900	            mapPropertyFromAPI(prop),
   901	          );
   902	        } else if (resultsArray && typeof resultsArray === "object") {
   903	          mlsResults = [mapPropertyFromAPI(resultsArray)];
   904	        }
   905	      } catch (error) {
   906	        console.warn(
   907	          "Comparison API failed, falling back to individual fetches:",
   908	          error,
   909	        );
   910	        const properties = await Promise.all(
   911	          mlsKeys.map((key) => fetchPropertyByKey(key)),
   912	        );
   913	        mlsResults = properties.filter((p) => p !== null) as Property[];
   914	      }
   915	    }
   916	
   917	    const finalResults = [...preConResults, ...estateResults, ...mlsResults];
   918	
   919	    return { results: finalResults, count: finalResults.length };
   920	  } catch (error) {
   921	    console.error("Error in fetchCompareProperties:", error);
   922	    return { results: [], count: 0 };
   923	  }
   924	}
   925	
   926	/**
   927	 * Fetch pre-construction properties
   928	 */
   929	export async function fetchPreConnProperties(
   930	  filters?: PreConnPropertyFilterParams,
   931	): Promise<{
   932	  results: any[];
   933	  count: number;
   934	  next: number | null;
   935	  previous: number | null;
   936	}> {
   937	  try {
   938	    const queryParams = new URLSearchParams();
   939	    const limit = filters?.limit || 6;
   940	    const offset = filters?.offset || 0;
   941	
   942	    queryParams.append("limit", limit.toString());
   943	    queryParams.append("offset", offset.toString());
   944	
   945	    if (filters) {
   946	      Object.entries(filters).forEach(([key, value]) => {
   947	        if (key === "limit" || key === "offset") return;
   948	        if (value !== undefined && value !== null && value !== "") {
   949	          const queryKey = key === "property_sub_type" ? "property_type" : key;
   950	          if (typeof value === "boolean") {
   951	            queryParams.append(queryKey, value ? "true" : "false");
   952	          } else {
   953	            queryParams.append(queryKey, value.toString());
   954	          }
   955	        }
   956	      });
   957	    }
   958	
   959	    const url = `${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/properties/pre-conn-properties/${queryParams.toString() ? "?" + queryParams.toString() : ""}`;
   960	    const cacheKey = `precon:${queryParams.toString()}`;
   961	    const cached = getClientCachedResponse<{
   962	      results: any[];
   963	      count: number;
   964	      next: number | null;
   965	      previous: number | null;
   966	    }>(cacheKey);
   967	    if (cached) return cached;
   968	
   969	    const response = await fetchAPI<{
   970	      results: any[];
   971	      count: number;
   972	      next: number | null;
   973	      previous: number | null;
   974	    }>(url, { cache: "no-store" });
   975	    const normalizedResponse = {
   976	      ...response,
   977	      results: (response.results || []).map((row) => mapPropertyFromAPI(row)),
   978	    };
   979	    setClientCachedResponse(cacheKey, normalizedResponse);
   980	    return normalizedResponse;
   981	  } catch (error) {
   982	    console.error("Error fetching pre-construction properties:", error);
   983	    return { results: [], count: 0, next: null, previous: null };
   984	  }
   985	}

   987	export async function fetchCommunityProperties(
   988	  filters?: CommunityPropertyFilterParams,
   989	): Promise<PaginatedPropertyResult> {
   990	  try {
   991	    const queryParams = new URLSearchParams();
   992	    const limit = filters?.limit || 12;
   993	    const offset = filters?.offset || 0;
   994	
   995	    queryParams.append("limit", limit.toString());
   996	    queryParams.append("offset", offset.toString());
   997	
   998	    if (filters) {
   999	      Object.entries(filters).forEach(([key, value]) => {
  1000	        if (key === "limit" || key === "offset") return;
  1001	        if (value !== undefined && value !== null && value !== "") {
  1002	          const queryKey = key === "property_sub_type" ? "property_type" : key;
  1003	          if (typeof value === "boolean") {
  1004	            queryParams.append(queryKey, value ? "true" : "false");
  1005	          } else {
  1006	            queryParams.append(queryKey, value.toString());
  1007	          }
  1008	        }
  1009	      });
  1010	    }
  1011	
  1012	    const url = `${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/properties/community-properties/${queryParams.toString() ? "?" + queryParams.toString() : ""}`;
  1013	    const cacheKey = `community:${queryParams.toString()}`;
  1014	    const cached = getClientCachedResponse<PaginatedPropertyResult>(cacheKey);
  1015	    if (cached) return cached;
  1016	
  1017	    const response = await fetchAPI<PaginatedPropertyResult>(url, {
  1018	      cache: "no-store",
  1019	    });
  1020	    const normalizedResponse: PaginatedPropertyResult = {
  1021	      ...response,
  1022	      results: (response.results || []).map((row) => mapPropertyFromAPI(row)),
  1023	    };
  1024	    setClientCachedResponse(cacheKey, normalizedResponse);
  1025	    return normalizedResponse;
  1026	  } catch (error) {
  1027	    console.error("Error fetching community properties:", error);
  1028	    return {
  1029	      results: [],
  1030	      count: 0,
  1031	      next: null,
  1032	      previous: null,
  1033	      fallback_applied: false,
  1034	      fallback_stage: null,
  1035	      suggested_locations: [],
  1036	    };
  1037	  }
  1038	}

  1055	/**
  1056	 * Fetch newly listed properties
  1057	 */
  1058	export async function fetchNewlyListedProperties(
  1059	  filters?: PropertyFilterParams & { days_threshold?: number },
  1060	): Promise<{
  1061	  results: any[];
  1062	  count: number;
  1063	  next: number | null;
  1064	  previous: number | null;
  1065	}> {
  1066	  const queryParams = new URLSearchParams();
  1067	  const limit = filters?.limit || 6;
  1068	  const offset = filters?.offset || 0;
  1069	
  1070	  queryParams.append("limit", limit.toString());
  1071	  queryParams.append("offset", offset.toString());
  1072	
  1073	  if (filters?.days_threshold) {
  1074	    queryParams.append("days_threshold", filters.days_threshold.toString());
  1075	  }
  1076	
  1077	  if (filters) {
  1078	    Object.entries(filters).forEach(([key, value]) => {
  1079	      if (key === "limit" || key === "offset" || key === "days_threshold")
  1080	        return;
  1081	      if (value !== undefined && value !== null && value !== "") {
  1082	        const queryKey = key === "property_sub_type" ? "property_type" : key;
  1083	        if (typeof value === "boolean") {
  1084	          queryParams.append(queryKey, value ? "true" : "false");
  1085	        } else {
  1086	          queryParams.append(queryKey, value.toString());
  1087	        }
  1088	      }
  1089	    });
  1090	  }
  1091	
  1092	  const url = `${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/properties/newly-listed-properties/${queryParams.toString() ? "?" + queryParams.toString() : ""}`;
  1093	  const cacheKey = `newly-listed:${queryParams.toString()}`;
  1094	  const cached = getClientCachedResponse<{
  1095	    results: any[];
  1096	    count: number;
  1097	    next: number | null;
  1098	    previous: number | null;
  1099	  }>(cacheKey);
  1100	  if (cached) return cached;
  1101	
  1102	  const response = await fetchAPI<{
  1103	    results: any[];
  1104	    count: number;
  1105	    next: number | null;
  1106	    previous: number | null;
  1107	  }>(url, { cache: "no-store" });
  1108	  setClientCachedResponse(cacheKey, response);
  1109	  return response;
  1110	}

  1157	/**
  1158	 * Fetch similar properties based on city, price range, and property type
  1159	 */
  1160	export async function fetchSimilarProperties(
  1161	  property: Property,
  1162	  limit: number = 4,
  1163	): Promise<Property[]> {
  1164	  try {
  1165	    const city = property.city || property.City;
  1166	    const propertyType =
  1167	      property.property_sub_type ||
  1168	      property.PropertySubType ||
  1169	      property.PropertyType;
  1170	    const price =
  1171	      typeof property.list_price === "string"
  1172	        ? parseFloat(property.list_price)
  1173	        : (property.list_price as number) || (property.ListPrice as number);
  1174	
  1175	    if (!city) return [];
  1176	
  1177	    const currentId = property.listing_key || property.ListingKey;
  1178	    const fetchCandidates = async (
  1179	      filters: Record<string, any>,
  1180	    ): Promise<Property[]> => {
  1181	      const data = await fetchFilteredProperties({
  1182	        ...filters,
  1183	        limit: limit + 12, // fetch enough headroom for de-dup + self filtering
  1184	      });
  1185	      const results = (data.results || []).map(mapPropertyFromAPI);
  1186	      return results.filter(
  1187	        (p: Property) => (p.listing_key || p.ListingKey) !== currentId,
  1188	      );
  1189	    };
  1190	
  1191	    const mergeUnique = (acc: Property[], incoming: Property[]) => {
  1192	      const seen = new Set(
  1193	        acc.map((p) => String(p.listing_key || p.ListingKey || "")),
  1194	      );
  1195	      for (const item of incoming) {
  1196	        const key = String(item.listing_key || item.ListingKey || "");
  1197	        if (!key || seen.has(key)) continue;
  1198	        acc.push(item);
  1199	        seen.add(key);
  1200	        if (acc.length >= limit) break;
  1201	      }
  1202	      return acc;
  1203	    };
  1204	
  1205	    // Fallback chain:
  1206	    // 1) strict: city + type + ±20%
  1207	    // 2) relaxed price: city + type + ±35%
  1208	    // 3) relaxed type: city + ±35%
  1209	    // 4) broad city-only
  1210	    const strictFilters: Record<string, any> = { city };
  1211	    if (propertyType) strictFilters.property_type = propertyType;
  1212	    if (price) {
  1213	      strictFilters.price_min = price * 0.8;
  1214	      strictFilters.price_max = price * 1.2;
  1215	    }
  1216	
  1217	    const relaxedPriceFilters: Record<string, any> = { city };
  1218	    if (propertyType) relaxedPriceFilters.property_type = propertyType;
  1219	    if (price) {
  1220	      relaxedPriceFilters.price_min = price * 0.65;
  1221	      relaxedPriceFilters.price_max = price * 1.35;
  1222	    }
  1223	
  1224	    const relaxedTypeFilters: Record<string, any> = { city };
  1225	    if (price) {
  1226	      relaxedTypeFilters.price_min = price * 0.65;
  1227	      relaxedTypeFilters.price_max = price * 1.35;
  1228	    }
  1229	
  1230	    const cityOnlyFilters: Record<string, any> = { city };
  1231	
  1232	    const buckets = await Promise.all([
  1233	      fetchCandidates(strictFilters),
  1234	      fetchCandidates(relaxedPriceFilters),
  1235	      fetchCandidates(relaxedTypeFilters),
  1236	      fetchCandidates(cityOnlyFilters),
  1237	    ]);
  1238	
  1239	    let finalResults: Property[] = [];
  1240	    for (const bucket of buckets) {
  1241	      finalResults = mergeUnique(finalResults, bucket);
  1242	      if (finalResults.length >= limit) break;
  1243	    }
  1244	
  1245	    return finalResults.slice(0, limit);
  1246	  } catch (error) {
  1247	    console.error("Error fetching similar properties:", error);
  1248	    return [];
  1249	  }
  1250	}
  1251	
  1252	export async function fetchRecommendationsForListing(
  1253	  property: Property,
  1254	  limit: number = 6,
  1255	): Promise<ListingRecommendationsResponse> {
  1256	  const listingKey =
  1257	    property.listing_key || property.ListingKey || property.PropertyKey;
  1258	  if (!listingKey) {
  1259	    return {
  1260	      for_this_home: [],
  1261	      based_on_your_history: [],
  1262	      people_also_viewed: [],
  1263	      fallback: [],
  1264	      metadata: { fallback_applied: true, reason: "missing_listing_key" },
  1265	    };
  1266	  }
  1267	
  1268	  // Recommendations endpoint currently supports MLS listing keys.
  1269	  // Estate/precon synthetic keys should skip this call to avoid noisy 404s.
  1270	  if (
  1271	    String(listingKey).startsWith("estate_") ||
  1272	    String(listingKey).startsWith("precon_")
  1273	  ) {
  1274	    return {
  1275	      for_this_home: [],
  1276	      based_on_your_history: [],
  1277	      people_also_viewed: [],
  1278	      fallback: [],
  1279	      metadata: { fallback_applied: true, reason: "unsupported_listing_type" },
  1280	    };
  1281	  }
  1282	
  1283	  try {
  1284	    const url = `${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/properties/${encodeURIComponent(String(listingKey))}/recommendations/?limit=${limit}`;
  1285	    const response = await fetchAPI<ListingRecommendationsResponse>(url, {
  1286	      cache: "no-store",
  1287	    });
  1288	    const normalize = (rows?: any[]) =>
  1289	      Array.isArray(rows)
  1290	        ? rows.map((row) => ({
  1291	            ...row,
  1292	            property: mapPropertyFromAPI(row.property),
  1293	          }))
  1294	        : [];
  1295	
  1296	    return {
  1297	      for_this_home: normalize(response.for_this_home),
  1298	      based_on_your_history: normalize(response.based_on_your_history),
  1299	      people_also_viewed: normalize(response.people_also_viewed),
  1300	      fallback: normalize(response.fallback),
  1301	      metadata: response.metadata || {},
  1302	    };
  1303	  } catch (error: any) {
  1304	    const msg = String(error?.message || "");
  1305	    if (msg.includes("API_ERROR:404")) {
  1306	      return {
  1307	        for_this_home: [],
  1308	        based_on_your_history: [],
  1309	        people_also_viewed: [],
  1310	        fallback: [],
  1311	        metadata: { fallback_applied: true, reason: "listing_not_found" },
  1312	      };
  1313	    }
  1314	    console.error("Error fetching listing recommendations:", error);
  1315	    return {
  1316	      for_this_home: [],
  1317	      based_on_your_history: [],
  1318	      people_also_viewed: [],
  1319	      fallback: [],
  1320	      metadata: { fallback_applied: true, reason: "request_failed" },
  1321	    };
  1322	  }
  1323	}
  1324	
  1325	export type ListingCatalogStatsPayload = {
  1326	  scope: { city: string | null; fsa: string | null };
  1327	  sample_size: number;
  1328	  median_list_price: number | null;
  1329	  mean_list_price: number | null;
  1330	  min_list_price: number | null;
  1331	  max_list_price: number | null;
  1332	  median_price_per_sqft: number | null;
  1333	  disclaimer: string;
  1334	};
  1335	
  1336	export async function fetchListingCatalogStats(params: {
  1337	  city?: string;
  1338	  fsa?: string;
  1339	}): Promise<ListingCatalogStatsPayload | null> {
  1340	  try {
  1341	    const usp = new URLSearchParams();
  1342	    if (params.city) usp.set("city", params.city);
  1343	    if (params.fsa) usp.set("fsa", params.fsa);
  1344	    const q = usp.toString();
  1345	    if (!q) return null;
  1346	    const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/catalog-stats/?${q}`, {
  1347	      next: { revalidate: 300 },
  1348	    });

  1457	export async function fetchListingTrends(params: {
  1458	  city?: string;
  1459	  fsa?: string;
  1460	  window?: "3m" | "6m" | "12m" | "24m";
  1461	}): Promise<ListingTrendsResponse | null> {
  1462	  try {
  1463	    const usp = new URLSearchParams();
  1464	    if (params.city) usp.set("city", params.city);
  1465	    if (params.fsa) usp.set("fsa", params.fsa);
  1466	    usp.set("window", params.window || "12m");
  1467	    const q = usp.toString();
  1468	    if (!q) return null;
  1469	    const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE_URL}/api/mls/trends/?${q}`, {
  1470	      next: { revalidate: 300 },
  1471	    });
  1472	    if (!res.ok) return null;
  1473	    return (await res.json()) as ListingTrendsResponse;
  1474	  } catch {
  1475	    return null;
  1476	  }
  1477	}

FILE: frontend/lib/api/client.ts

     1	// lib/api/client.ts
     2	
     3	import { env } from "../env";
     4	
     5	export const API_BASE_URL = env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL;
     6	
     7	export class ApiError extends Error {
     8	  constructor(
     9	    public readonly status: number,
    10	    public readonly responseBody: string,
    11	  ) {
    12	    super(`API_ERROR:${status}:${responseBody}`);
    13	    this.name = "ApiError";
    14	  }
    15	}
    16	
    17	export function isApiError(error: unknown): error is ApiError {
    18	  return error instanceof ApiError;
    19	}
    20	
    21	function isDynamicServerUsageError(error: unknown): boolean {
    22	  if (!(error instanceof Error)) return false;
    23	  const digest = "digest" in error ? error.digest : undefined;
    24	  return (
    25	    digest === "DYNAMIC_SERVER_USAGE" ||
    26	    error.message.includes("DYNAMIC_SERVER_USAGE")
    27	  );
    28	}
    29	
    30	/**
    31	 * Enhanced fetch wrapper with better error handling
    32	 */
    33	export async function fetchAPI<T>(
    34	  url: string,
    35	  options?: RequestInit,
    36	): Promise<T> {
    37	  try {
    38	    const response = await fetch(url, {
    39	      ...options,
    40	      headers: {
    41	        "Content-Type": "application/json",
    42	        ...((typeof window !== "undefined" && localStorage.getItem("access_token"))
    43	          ? { Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem("access_token")}` }
    44	          : {}),
    45	        ...options?.headers,
    46	      },
    47	    });
    48	
    49	    // console.log(`API Request: ${url} - Status: ${response.status}`);
    50	
    51	    if (!response.ok) {
    52	      // Read body exactly once to avoid "body stream already read" errors.
    53	      const rawErrorBody = await response.text();
    54	      let errorData: unknown = rawErrorBody;
    55	      if (rawErrorBody) {
    56	        try {
    57	          errorData = JSON.parse(rawErrorBody);
    58	        } catch {
    59	          errorData = rawErrorBody;
    60	        }
    61	      }
    62	
    63	      const errorMessage =
    64	        typeof errorData === "object"
    65	          ? JSON.stringify(errorData)
    66	          : String(errorData ?? "");
    67	
    68	      // Only log as error if it's not a common "not found" scenario which the caller might handle
    69	      if (
    70	        response.status !== 404 &&
    71	        !errorMessage.includes("404") &&
    72	        !errorMessage.includes("not exist") &&
    73	        !errorMessage.includes("primary key is invalid")
    74	      ) {
    75	        console.error(`API Error ${response.status}: ${errorMessage}`);
    76	      } else {
    77	        console.warn(
    78	          `API Reference Error ${response.status}: Resource might not exist or key is invalid.`,
    79	        );
    80	      }
    81	
    82	      throw new ApiError(response.status, errorMessage);
    83	    }
    84	
    85	    const data = await response.json();
    86	    return data;
    87	  } catch (error: unknown) {
    88	    // Avoid double logging if it's already logged above
    89	    if (error instanceof Error && !error.message.startsWith("API_ERROR:")) {
    90	      // Ignore Next.js dynamic server usage errors (bailouts from static generation)
    91	      if (isDynamicServerUsageError(error)) {
    92	        throw error;
    93	      }
    94	      console.error(`Network error fetching ${url}:`, error);
    95	    }
    96	    throw error;
    97	  }
    98	}
