    65	function parseJsonLike(value: unknown): JsonMap {
    66	  if (value && typeof value === "object" && !Array.isArray(value)) {
    67	    return value as JsonMap;
    68	  }
    69	  if (typeof value !== "string") return {};
    70	  try {
    71	    const parsed = JSON.parse(value);
    72	    return parsed && typeof parsed === "object" && !Array.isArray(parsed)
    73	      ? (parsed as JsonMap)
    74	      : {};
    75	  } catch {
    76	    return {};
    77	  }
    78	}
    79	
    80	function parseDescriptionSections(value: unknown): Array<{
    81	  id: string;
    82	  title: string;
    83	  body_html: string;
    84	  order: number;
    85	}> {
    86	  let rawArray: unknown[] = [];
    87	  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    88	    rawArray = value;
    89	  } else if (typeof value === "string") {
    90	    try {
    91	      const parsed = JSON.parse(value);
    92	      if (Array.isArray(parsed)) {
    93	        rawArray = parsed;
    94	      }
    95	    } catch {
    96	      rawArray = [];
    97	    }
    98	  }
    99	
   100	  return rawArray
   101	    .map((item, idx) => {
   102	      if (!item || typeof item !== "object") return null;
   103	      const typed = item as JsonMap;
   104	      return {
   105	        id: toCleanString(typed.id) || `section-${idx + 1}`,
   106	        title: toCleanString(typed.title),
   107	        body_html: toCleanString(typed.body_html),
   108	        order:
   109	          typeof typed.order === "number"
   110	            ? typed.order
   111	            : Number.parseInt(String(typed.order ?? idx), 10) || idx,
   112	      };
   113	    })
   114	    .filter(
   115	      (
   116	        section,
   117	      ): section is {
   118	        id: string;
   119	        title: string;
   120	        body_html: string;
   121	        order: number;
   122	      } => Boolean(section),
   123	    )
   124	    .sort((a, b) => a.order - b.order);
   125	}
   126	
   127	function getFirstDescriptionSectionBody(value: unknown): string {
   128	  const sections = parseDescriptionSections(value);
   129	  return sections[0]?.body_html || "";
   130	}
   131	
   132	function unwrapMetaValue(value: unknown): unknown {
   133	  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
   134	    for (const item of value) {
   135	      const nested = unwrapMetaValue(item);
   136	      if (nested !== null && nested !== undefined && toCleanString(nested)) {
   137	        return nested;
   138	      }
   139	    }
   140	    return value.length > 0 ? value[0] : undefined;
   141	  }
   142	  return value;
   143	}
   144	
   145	function wpMetaValue(wpMeta: JsonMap, ...keys: string[]): unknown {
   146	  for (const key of keys) {
   147	    if (!(key in wpMeta)) continue;
   148	    let raw = unwrapMetaValue(wpMeta[key]);
   149	    if (raw && typeof raw === "object" && !Array.isArray(raw)) {
   150	      const objectLike = raw as JsonMap;
   151	      raw =
   152	        objectLike.rendered ??
   153	        objectLike.value ??
   154	        objectLike.url ??
   155	        objectLike.name ??
   156	        undefined;
   157	    }
   158	    if (raw === null || raw === undefined) continue;
   159	    if (typeof raw === "string" && raw.trim() === "") continue;
   160	    return raw;
   161	  }
   162	  return undefined;
   163	}
   164	
   165	function taxonomyLabel(wpTerms: JsonMap, ...keys: string[]): string {
   166	  for (const key of keys) {
   167	    const raw = unwrapMetaValue(wpTerms[key]);
   168	    const value = toCleanString(raw);
   169	    if (value) return value;
   170	  }
   171	  return "";
   172	}
   173	
   174	function toNumberLoose(value: unknown): number | undefined {
   175	  if (value == null || value === "") return undefined;
   176	  if (typeof value === "number")
   177	    return Number.isFinite(value) ? value : undefined;
   178	  const parsed = Number(String(value).replace(/[^0-9.-]+/g, ""));
   179	  return Number.isFinite(parsed) ? parsed : undefined;
   180	}
   181	
   182	function parseLatLngPair(value: unknown): { lat?: number; lng?: number } {
   183	  const text = toCleanString(unwrapMetaValue(value));
   184	  if (!text) return {};
   185	  const parts = text.split(/[,\s|]+/).filter(Boolean);
   186	  if (parts.length < 2) return {};
   187	  const lat = toNumberLoose(parts[0]);
   188	  const lng = toNumberLoose(parts[1]);
   189	  return { lat, lng };
   190	}
   191	
   192	function inferCityFromAddress(value: unknown): string {
   193	  const text = toCleanString(value);
   194	  if (!text) return "";
   195	  const parts = text
   196	    .split(",")
   197	    .map((p) => p.trim())
   198	    .filter(Boolean);
   199	  if (parts.length < 2) return "";
   200	  return parts[parts.length - 2] || "";
   201	}
   202	
   203	function inferProvinceFromAddress(value: unknown): string {
   204	  const text = toCleanString(value);
   205	  if (!text) return "";
   206	  const parts = text
   207	    .split(",")
   208	    .map((p) => p.trim())
   209	    .filter(Boolean);
   210	  if (parts.length === 0) return "";
   211	  const tail = parts[parts.length - 1];
   212	  const codeMatch = tail.match(/\b([A-Z]{2})\b/);
   213	  if (codeMatch?.[1]) return codeMatch[1];
   214	  return tail;
   215	}
   216	
   217	function toCleanString(value: unknown): string {
   218	  if (value == null) return "";
   219	  const text = String(value).trim();
   220	  if (!text) return "";
   221	  if (text.startsWith("/media/")) {
   222	    const base = String(API_BASE_URL || "").trim().replace(/\/+$/, "");
   223	    return base ? `${base}${text}` : text;
   224	  }
   225	  return text;
   226	}
   227	
   228	function firstString(...values: unknown[]): string {
   229	  for (const value of values) {
   230	    const str = toCleanString(value);
   231	    if (str) return str;
   232	  }
   233	  return "";
   234	}
   235	
   236	function cleanHtml(value: unknown): string {
   237	  return toCleanString(value)
   238	    .replace(/<[^>]*>/g, " ")
   239	    .replace(/&nbsp;/gi, " ")
   240	    .replace(/\s+/g, " ")
   241	    .trim();
   242	}
   243	
   244	function toNumberOrOriginal(value: unknown): number | string | null {
   245	  if (value == null || value === "") return null;
   246	  if (typeof value === "number") return Number.isFinite(value) ? value : null;
   247	  const cleaned = String(value).replace(/[^0-9.-]+/g, "");
   248	  if (!cleaned) return String(value);
   249	  const parsed = Number(cleaned);
   250	  return Number.isFinite(parsed) ? parsed : String(value);
   251	}
   252	
   253	function toNumberSafe(value: unknown): number {
   254	  const normalized = toNumberOrOriginal(value);
   255	  if (typeof normalized === "number" && Number.isFinite(normalized)) {
   256	    return normalized;
   257	  }
   258	  if (typeof normalized === "string") {
   259	    const parsed = Number(normalized.replace(/[^0-9.-]+/g, ""));
   260	    return Number.isFinite(parsed) ? parsed : 0;
   261	  }
   262	  return 0;
   263	}
   264	
   265	function looksLikeImageUrl(value: string): boolean {
   266	  if (!value) return false;
   267	  const normalized = value.toLowerCase();
   268	  if (normalized.startsWith("http://") || normalized.startsWith("https://")) {
   269	    return true;
   270	  }
   271	  return /\.(png|jpe?g|webp|gif|avif|svg)(\?.*)?$/i.test(normalized);
   272	}
   273	
   274	function isAllowedRemoteUrl(value: string): boolean {
   275	  try {
   276	    const url = new URL(value);
   277	    if (!["http:", "https:"].includes(url.protocol)) return false;
   278	    return NEXT_ALLOWED_IMAGE_HOSTS.has(url.hostname);
   279	  } catch {
   280	    return false;
   281	  }
   282	}
   283	
   284	function filenameFromUrl(url: string): string | null {
   285	  if (!url) return null;
   286	  try {
   287	    const parsed = new URL(url, "https://placeholder.invalid");
   288	    const segments = parsed.pathname.split("/").filter(Boolean);
   289	    if (segments.length === 0) return null;
   290	    return decodeURIComponent(segments[segments.length - 1]) || null;
   291	  } catch {
   292	    return null;
   293	  }
   294	}
   295	
   296	function extractCandidateStrings(
   297	  value: unknown,
   298	  out: string[],
   299	  depth = 0,
   300	): void {
   301	  if (depth > 3 || value == null) return;
   302	
   303	  if (typeof value === "string") {
   304	    const text = value.trim();
   305	    if (looksLikeImageUrl(text)) out.push(text);
   306	    return;
   307	  }
   308	
   309	  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
   310	    for (const entry of value) {
   311	      extractCandidateStrings(entry, out, depth + 1);
   312	    }
   313	    return;
   314	  }
   315	
   316	  if (typeof value === "object") {
   317	    for (const [key, entry] of Object.entries(value as JsonMap)) {
   318	      if (/image|photo|gallery|media/i.test(key)) {
   319	        extractCandidateStrings(entry, out, depth + 1);
   320	      }
   321	    }
   322	  }
   323	}
   324	
   325	function pickImageValue(item: unknown): string {
   326	  if (!item) return "";
   327	  if (typeof item === "string") return item.trim();
   328	  if (typeof item !== "object") return "";
   329	
   330	  const typed = item as JsonMap;
   331	  for (const key of IMAGE_OBJECT_KEYS) {
   332	    const value = toCleanString(typed[key]);
   333	    if (value) return value;
   334	  }
   335	  return "";
   336	}
   337	
   338	function getRawMediaCandidates(
   339	  prop: JsonMap,
   340	  wpMeta: JsonMap,
   341	  wpPost: JsonMap,
   342	): string[] {
   343	  const candidates: string[] = [];
   344	  const push = (value: string) => {
   345	    const cleaned = toCleanString(value);
   346	    if (!cleaned || !looksLikeImageUrl(cleaned)) return;
   347	    // Prevent runtime crashes in next/image by keeping only configured remote hosts.
   348	    if (cleaned.startsWith("http://") || cleaned.startsWith("https://")) {
   349	      if (!isAllowedRemoteUrl(cleaned)) return;
   350	    }
   351	    candidates.push(cleaned);
   352	  };
   353	
   354	  const mediaCollections = [
   355	    prop.media,
   356	    prop.Media,
   357	    prop.photos,
   358	    prop.Photos,
   359	    prop.images,
   360	    prop.Images,
   361	    wpPost.media,
   362	    wpPost.Media,
   363	    wpPost.images,
   364	    wpPost.gallery,
   365	  ];
   366	
   367	  for (const collection of mediaCollections) {
   368	    if (!collection) continue;
   369	    if (Array.isArray(collection)) {
   370	      for (const item of collection) {
   371	        const url = pickImageValue(item);
   372	        if (url) push(url);
   373	      }
   374	    } else {
   375	      const url = pickImageValue(collection);
   376	      if (url) push(url);
   377	    }
   378	  }
   379	
   380	  for (const key of IMAGE_DIRECT_KEYS) {
   381	    push(toCleanString(prop[key]));
   382	    push(toCleanString(wpPost[key]));
   383	  }
   384	
   385	  const yoast = wpPost.yoast_head_json as JsonMap | undefined;
   386	  if (yoast && Array.isArray((yoast as JsonMap).og_image)) {
   387	    for (const image of (yoast as JsonMap).og_image as unknown[]) {
   388	      const url = pickImageValue(image);
   389	      if (url) push(url);
   390	    }
   391	  }
   392	
   393	  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(wpMeta)) {
   394	    if (/image|photo|gallery|media/i.test(key)) {
   395	      const nested: string[] = [];
   396	      extractCandidateStrings(value, nested);
   397	      nested.forEach(push);
   398	    }
   399	  }
   400	
   401	  const unique = new Set<string>();
   402	  const ordered: string[] = [];
   403	  for (const item of candidates) {
   404	    if (!unique.has(item)) {
   405	      unique.add(item);
   406	      ordered.push(item);
   407	    }
   408	  }
   409	  return ordered;
   410	}
   411	
   412	function buildMedia(urls: string[]): PropertyMedia[] {
   413	  return urls.map((url, index) => ({
   414	    media_url: url,
   415	    media_category: "Property Photo",
   416	    is_preferred: index === 0,
   417	    order: index + 1,
   418	    image_filename: filenameFromUrl(url) || undefined,
   419	  })) as PropertyMedia[];
   420	}
   421	
   422	function normalizeRoomsArray(value: unknown): unknown[] {
   423	  if (Array.isArray(value)) return value;
   424	  if (typeof value === "string") {
   425	    const trimmed = value.trim();
   426	    if (!trimmed) return [];
   427	    try {
   428	      const parsed = JSON.parse(trimmed);
   429	      return Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed : [];
   430	    } catch {
   431	      return [];
   432	    }
   433	  }
   434	  return [];
   435	}
   436	
   437	export function normalizeListingRecord(
   438	  rawProp: unknown,
   439	  options: NormalizeListingOptions = {},
   440	): Property {
   441	  const prop = ((rawProp as JsonMap) || {}) as JsonMap;
   442	  const wpMeta = parseJsonLike(prop.wp_meta_json);
   443	  const wpPost = parseJsonLike(prop.wp_post_json);
   444	
   445	  const normalizedCity =
   446	    firstString(prop.city, prop.City, prop.location, options.defaultCity) ||
   447	    "Unknown City";
   448	  const normalizedProvince = firstString(
   449	    prop.state_or_province,
   450	    prop.StateOrProvince,
   451	    prop.province,
   452	    wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_state"),
   453	  );
   454	  const normalizedStatus =
   455	    firstString(
   456	      prop.standard_status,
   457	      prop.StandardStatus,
   458	      prop.publish_status,
   459	      wpPost.post_status,
   460	      options.defaultStatus,
   461	    ) || "For Sale";
   462	  const normalizedType =
   463	    firstString(
   464	      prop.property_sub_type,
   465	      prop.PropertySubType,
   466	      prop.PropertyType,
   467	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_type"),
   468	      options.defaultType,
   469	    ) || "Property";
   470	
   471	  const forcedKey = options.forceListingKey;
   472	  const bestKey =
   473	    firstString(
   474	      forcedKey,
   475	      prop.listing_key,
   476	      prop.ListingKey,
   477	      prop.PropertyKey,
   478	      prop.listing_id,
   479	      prop.id,
   480	    ) || `property-${normalizedCity.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, "-")}`;
   481	
   482	  const title =
   483	    firstString(
   484	      prop.project_name,
   485	      prop.property_title,
   486	      prop.title,
   487	      (wpPost.title as JsonMap | undefined)?.rendered,
   488	      prop.unparsed_address,
   489	      prop.address,
   490	      prop.street_name,
   491	      bestKey,
   492	      options.defaultTitle,
   493	    ) || "Listing";
   494	
   495	  const description = cleanHtml(
   496	    firstString(
   497	      getFirstDescriptionSectionBody(prop.description_sections_json),
   498	      prop.property_description,
   499	      prop.public_remarks,
   500	      prop.PublicRemarks,
   501	      (wpPost.content as JsonMap | undefined)?.rendered,
   502	      wpPost.excerpt,
   503	    ),
   504	  );
   505	
   506	  const images = getRawMediaCandidates(prop, wpMeta, wpPost);
   507	  const media = buildMedia(images);
   508	  const primaryImage = media[0]?.media_url || "";
   509	  const imageFilename = filenameFromUrl(primaryImage) || "";
   510	
   511	  const rawPrice =
   512	    prop.list_price ??
   513	    prop.ListPrice ??
   514	    wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_price", "sale_or_rent_price");
   515	  const rawBeds =
   516	    prop.bedrooms_total ??
   517	    prop.BedroomsTotal ??
   518	    wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_bedrooms");
   519	  const rawBaths =
   520	    prop.bathrooms_total_integer ??
   521	    prop.BathroomsTotalInteger ??
   522	    wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_bathrooms");
   523	  const rawSqft =
   524	    prop.building_area_total ??
   525	    prop.LivingArea ??
   526	    prop.living_area ??
   527	    wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_size");
   528	  const normalizedRooms = normalizeRoomsArray(prop.rooms);
   529	  const normalizedLegacyRooms = normalizeRoomsArray(prop.Rooms);
   530	  const resolvedRooms = normalizedRooms.length
   531	    ? normalizedRooms
   532	    : normalizedLegacyRooms;
   533	
   534	  return {
   535	    ...(prop as Property),
   536	    id: firstString(prop.id),
   537	    listing_key: bestKey,
   538	    ListingKey: bestKey,
   539	    PropertyKey: bestKey,
   540	    listing_id: firstString(prop.listing_id, prop.listing_key, bestKey),
   541	    project_name: title,
   542	    property_title: firstString(prop.property_title, title),
   543	    address: firstString(prop.address, prop.unparsed_address, title),
   544	    unparsed_address: firstString(prop.unparsed_address, prop.address, title),
   545	    city: normalizedCity,
   546	    City: normalizedCity,
   547	    state_or_province: firstString(
   548	      prop.state_or_province,
   549	      prop.StateOrProvince,
   550	      prop.province,
   551	      normalizedProvince,
   552	    ),
   553	    StateOrProvince: firstString(
   554	      prop.StateOrProvince,
   555	      prop.state_or_province,
   556	      prop.province,
   557	      normalizedProvince,
   558	    ),
   559	    province: firstString(prop.province, normalizedProvince),
   560	    postal_code: firstString(
   561	      prop.postal_code,
   562	      prop.PostalCode,
   563	      prop.postalCode,
   564	    ),
   565	    PostalCode: firstString(
   566	      prop.PostalCode,
   567	      prop.postal_code,
   568	      prop.postalCode,
   569	    ),
   570	    location: firstString(prop.location, normalizedCity),
   571	    standard_status: normalizedStatus,
   572	    StandardStatus: normalizedStatus,
   573	    property_sub_type: normalizedType,
   574	    PropertySubType: normalizedType,
   575	    list_price: toNumberOrOriginal(rawPrice),
   576	    ListPrice: toNumberSafe(rawPrice),
   577	    bedrooms_total: toNumberOrOriginal(rawBeds),
   578	    BedroomsTotal: toNumberSafe(rawBeds),
   579	    bathrooms_total_integer: toNumberOrOriginal(rawBaths),
   580	    BathroomsTotalInteger: toNumberSafe(rawBaths),
   581	    building_area_total: toNumberOrOriginal(rawSqft),
   582	    total_actual_rent:
   583	      prop.total_actual_rent == null
   584	        ? undefined
   585	        : String(prop.total_actual_rent),
   586	    public_remarks: description,
   587	    PublicRemarks: description,
   588	    property_description: firstString(
   589	      prop.property_description,
   590	      getFirstDescriptionSectionBody(prop.description_sections_json),
   591	      description,
   592	    ),
   593	    description_sections_json: parseDescriptionSections(
   594	      prop.description_sections_json,
   595	    ),
   596	    custom_detail_blocks_json:
   597	      prop.custom_detail_blocks_json ?? wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "custom_detail_blocks_json"),
   598	    detail_blocks_layout_json:
   599	      prop.detail_blocks_layout_json ?? wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "detail_blocks_layout_json"),
   600	    listing_buttons_json:
   601	      prop.listing_buttons_json ?? wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "listing_buttons_json"),
   602	    rooms: resolvedRooms,
   603	    Rooms: resolvedRooms,
   604	    media,
   605	    Media: media,
   606	    featured_image_url: firstString(prop.featured_image_url, primaryImage),
   607	    primary_image_url: firstString(prop.primary_image_url, primaryImage),
   608	    image_filename: imageFilename,
   609	    image_names: media
   610	      .map((item) => (item as unknown as JsonMap).image_filename)
   611	      .filter((x): x is string => typeof x === "string" && x.length > 0),
   612	    modification_timestamp: firstString(
   613	      prop.modification_timestamp,
   614	      prop.ModificationTimestamp,
   615	    ),
   616	    ModificationTimestamp: firstString(
   617	      prop.ModificationTimestamp,
   618	      prop.modification_timestamp,
   619	      new Date().toISOString(),
   620	    ),
   621	  } as Property;
   622	}
   623	
   624	export function normalizeEstateDetailRecord(
   625	  rawProp: unknown,
   626	  id?: string,
   627	): Property {
   628	  const prop = ((rawProp as JsonMap) || {}) as JsonMap;
   629	  const key = `estate_${id || firstString(prop.id, prop.listing_key, prop.listing_id, "unknown")}`;
   630	
   631	  const wpMeta = parseJsonLike(prop.wp_meta_json);
   632	  const wpPost = parseJsonLike(prop.wp_post_json);
   633	  const wpTerms = parseJsonLike(prop.wp_terms_json);
   634	  const fallbackCoords = parseLatLngPair(
   635	    wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_location"),
   636	  );
   637	  const fallbackType = taxonomyLabel(wpTerms, "type", "property_type");
   638	  const fallbackStatus = taxonomyLabel(wpTerms, "status", "property_status");
   639	  const fallbackCountry = taxonomyLabel(wpTerms, "country");
   640	  const fallbackAddress = firstString(
   641	    prop.unparsed_address,
   642	    prop.address,
   643	    wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_address", "fave_property_map_address"),
   644	  );
   645	  const fallbackCity = inferCityFromAddress(fallbackAddress);
   646	  const fallbackProvince = inferProvinceFromAddress(fallbackAddress);
   647	  const fallbackTitle = firstString(
   648	    prop.property_title,
   649	    prop.project_name,
   650	    (wpPost.title as JsonMap | undefined)?.rendered,
   651	    wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "post_title", "title"),
   652	    prop.unparsed_address,
   653	    key,
   654	  );
   655	
   656	  const enriched = {
   657	    ...prop,
   658	    id: firstString(prop.id, id),
   659	    listing_key: key,
   660	    ListingKey: key,
   661	    PropertyKey: key,
   662	    project_name: firstString(
   663	      prop.project_name,
   664	      prop.property_title,
   665	      (wpPost.title as JsonMap | undefined)?.rendered,
   666	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "post_title", "title"),
   667	      prop.unparsed_address,
   668	      key,
   669	    ),
   670	    property_title: firstString(
   671	      prop.property_title,
   672	      prop.project_name,
   673	      (wpPost.title as JsonMap | undefined)?.rendered,
   674	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "post_title", "title"),
   675	      prop.unparsed_address,
   676	      key,
   677	    ),
   678	    title: firstString(
   679	      prop.title,
   680	      fallbackTitle,
   681	    ),
   682	    city: firstString(
   683	      prop.city,
   684	      prop.location,
   685	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_city"),
   686	      taxonomyLabel(wpTerms, "city", "property_city"),
   687	      fallbackCity,
   688	    ),
   689	    City: firstString(
   690	      prop.City,
   691	      prop.city,
   692	      prop.location,
   693	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_city"),
   694	      taxonomyLabel(wpTerms, "city", "property_city"),
   695	      fallbackCity,
   696	    ),
   697	    state_or_province: firstString(
   698	      prop.state_or_province,
   699	      prop.province,
   700	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_state"),
   701	      prop.StateOrProvince,
   702	      taxonomyLabel(wpTerms, "state"),
   703	      fallbackProvince,
   704	    ),
   705	    StateOrProvince: firstString(
   706	      prop.StateOrProvince,
   707	      prop.state_or_province,
   708	      prop.province,
   709	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_state"),
   710	      taxonomyLabel(wpTerms, "state"),
   711	      fallbackProvince,
   712	    ),
   713	    province: firstString(
   714	      prop.province,
   715	      prop.state_or_province,
   716	      prop.StateOrProvince,
   717	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_state"),
   718	      taxonomyLabel(wpTerms, "state"),
   719	      fallbackProvince,
   720	    ),
   721	    standard_status: firstString(
   722	      prop.standard_status,
   723	      prop.publish_status,
   724	      fallbackStatus,
   725	      "For Sale",
   726	    ),
   727	    StandardStatus: firstString(
   728	      prop.StandardStatus,
   729	      prop.standard_status,
   730	      prop.publish_status,
   731	      fallbackStatus,
   732	      "For Sale",
   733	    ),
   734	    property_sub_type: firstString(
   735	      prop.property_sub_type,
   736	      prop.PropertySubType,
   737	      prop.PropertyType,
   738	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_type"),
   739	      fallbackType,
   740	      "Property",
   741	    ),
   742	    PropertySubType: firstString(
   743	      prop.PropertySubType,
   744	      prop.property_sub_type,
   745	      prop.PropertyType,
   746	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_type"),
   747	      fallbackType,
   748	      "Property",
   749	    ),
   750	    public_remarks: firstString(
   751	      prop.public_remarks,
   752	      prop.PublicRemarks,
   753	      getFirstDescriptionSectionBody(prop.description_sections_json),
   754	      prop.property_description,
   755	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "post_content", "description"),
   756	      (wpPost.content as JsonMap | undefined)?.rendered,
   757	      wpPost.excerpt,
   758	    ),
   759	    property_description: firstString(
   760	      getFirstDescriptionSectionBody(prop.description_sections_json),
   761	      prop.property_description,
   762	      prop.public_remarks,
   763	      prop.PublicRemarks,
   764	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "post_content", "description"),
   765	      (wpPost.content as JsonMap | undefined)?.rendered,
   766	      wpPost.excerpt,
   767	    ),
   768	    description_sections_json: parseDescriptionSections(
   769	      prop.description_sections_json,
   770	    ),
   771	    custom_detail_blocks_json:
   772	      prop.custom_detail_blocks_json ?? wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "custom_detail_blocks_json"),
   773	    detail_blocks_layout_json:
   774	      prop.detail_blocks_layout_json ?? wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "detail_blocks_layout_json"),
   775	    listing_buttons_json:
   776	      prop.listing_buttons_json ?? wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "listing_buttons_json"),
   777	    list_price:
   778	      prop.list_price ??
   779	      prop.ListPrice ??
   780	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_price", "sale_or_rent_price") ??
   781	      prop.second_price,
   782	    second_price:
   783	      prop.second_price ??
   784	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "second_price", "fave_property_sec_price"),
   785	    bedrooms_total:
   786	      prop.bedrooms_total ??
   787	      prop.BedroomsTotal ??
   788	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_bedrooms"),
   789	    bathrooms_total_integer:
   790	      prop.bathrooms_total_integer ??
   791	      prop.BathroomsTotalInteger ??
   792	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_bathrooms"),
   793	    building_area_total:
   794	      prop.building_area_total ??
   795	      prop.living_area ??
   796	      prop.LivingArea ??
   797	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_size"),
   798	    lot_size_dimensions: firstString(
   799	      prop.lot_size_dimensions,
   800	      prop.lot_size,
   801	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_lot_size"),
   802	    ),
   803	    lot_size: firstString(
   804	      prop.lot_size,
   805	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_lot_size"),
   806	    ),
   807	    land_area:
   808	      prop.land_area ?? wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_land", "land_area"),
   809	    land_area_size_postfix: firstString(
   810	      prop.land_area_size_postfix,
   811	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_land_postfix"),
   812	    ),
   813	    price_prefix: firstString(
   814	      prop.price_prefix,
   815	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_size_prefix", "price_prefix"),
   816	    ),
   817	    size_postfix: firstString(
   818	      prop.size_postfix,
   819	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_size_postfix", "size_postfix"),
   820	    ),
   821	    address: firstString(
   822	      prop.address,
   823	      prop.unparsed_address,
   824	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_address", "fave_property_map_address"),
   825	    ),
   826	    unparsed_address: firstString(
   827	      prop.unparsed_address,
   828	      prop.address,
   829	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_address", "fave_property_map_address"),
   830	    ),
   831	    postal_code: firstString(
   832	      prop.postal_code,
   833	      prop.PostalCode,
   834	      prop.postalCode,
   835	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_zip"),
   836	    ),
   837	    PostalCode: firstString(
   838	      prop.PostalCode,
   839	      prop.postal_code,
   840	      prop.postalCode,
   841	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_zip"),
   842	    ),
   843	    country: firstString(prop.country, fallbackCountry),
   844	    latitude:
   845	      prop.latitude ??
   846	      prop.Latitude ??
   847	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "houzez_geolocation_lat") ??
   848	      fallbackCoords.lat,
   849	    longitude:
   850	      prop.longitude ??
   851	      prop.Longitude ??
   852	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "houzez_geolocation_long") ??
   853	      fallbackCoords.lng,
   854	    listing_id: firstString(
   855	      prop.listing_id,
   856	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_mls-id", "fave_property_id"),
   857	      key,
   858	    ),
   859	    property_id_code: firstString(
   860	      prop.property_id_code,
   861	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_id", "property_id"),
   862	    ),
   863	    publish_status: firstString(prop.publish_status, wpPost.post_status),
   864	    listing_url: firstString(
   865	      prop.listing_url,
   866	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "permalink"),
   867	      wpPost.link,
   868	    ),
   869	    location: firstString(
   870	      prop.location,
   871	      prop.city,
   872	      prop.City,
   873	      fallbackCity,
   874	    ),
   875	    featured_image_url: firstString(
   876	      prop.featured_image_url,
   877	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "featured_image", "featured_image_url"),
   878	      wpPost.featured_image_url,
   879	    ),
   880	    developer: firstString(
   881	      prop.developer,
   882	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_developer", "developer"),
   883	    ),
   884	    occupancy_year:
   885	      prop.occupancy_year ??
   886	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_occupancy", "occupancy"),
   887	    year_built:
   888	      prop.year_built ?? prop.YearBuilt ?? wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "year_built"),
   889	    tax_annual_amount:
   890	      prop.tax_annual_amount ?? wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_taxes"),
   891	    tax_year: prop.tax_year ?? wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_tax-year"),
   892	    garages:
   893	      prop.garages ?? wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_garage", "garages"),
   894	    garage_size:
   895	      prop.garage_size ??
   896	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_garage_size", "garage_size"),
   897	    kitchens:
   898	      prop.kitchens ??
   899	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_kitchens", "kitchens"),
   900	    rooms: prop.rooms ?? wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_rooms"),
   901	    total_rooms:
   902	      prop.total_rooms ?? wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_property_rooms", "rooms"),
   903	    basement: firstString(prop.basement, wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_basement")),
   904	    exterior_features: firstString(
   905	      prop.exterior_features,
   906	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_exterior"),
   907	    ),
   908	    video_tour_url: firstString(
   909	      prop.video_tour_url,
   910	      prop.virtual_tour_url,
   911	      wpMetaValue(wpMeta, "fave_video_url", "video_url"),
   912	    ),
   913	    modification_timestamp: firstString(
   914	      prop.modification_timestamp,
   915	      prop.ModificationTimestamp,
   916	      wpPost.modified,
   917	      wpPost.date,
   918	    ),
   919	  };
   920	
   921	  return normalizeListingRecord(enriched, {
   922	    forceListingKey: key,
   923	    defaultStatus: "For Sale",
   924	    defaultCity: "Unknown City",
   925	    defaultType: "Property",
   926	    defaultTitle: "Estate Listing",
   927	  });
   928	}

     1	import { strict as assert } from "node:assert";

     8	describe("normalizeListingRecord", () => {
     9	  it("coerces null-like fields to schema-safe values", () => {
    10	    const normalized = normalizeListingRecord({
    11	      id: 9,
    12	      city: "Toronto",
    13	      list_price: 1200000,
    14	      total_actual_rent: null,
    15	      rooms: null,
    16	    });
    17	
    18	    assert.equal(normalized.id, "9");
    19	    assert.equal(normalized.total_actual_rent, undefined);
    20	    assert.deepEqual(normalized.rooms, []);
    21	    assert.deepEqual(normalized.Rooms, []);
    22	  });
    23	
    24	  it("extracts image names and keeps only configured remote hosts", () => {
    25	    const normalized = normalizeListingRecord({
    26	      id: 3,
    27	      city: "Toronto",
    28	      media: [
    29	        {
    30	          media_url:
    31	            "https://imgs.search.brave.com/udTxVRziGBr8NGtRoLftUpy--2c1lnzqkMUTgJkdgrs/rs:fit:860:0:0:0/g:ce/aHR0cHM6Ly9oaXBzLmhlYXJzdGFwcHMuY29tL2hvdXNlLmpwZw==",
    32	        },
    33	        {
    34	          media_url:
    35	            "https://estate-4u.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/sample-home.jpg?ver=1",
    36	        },
    37	      ],
    38	    });
    39	
    40	    const media = normalized.media || [];
    41	    assert.equal(media.length, 1);
    42	    assert.equal(
    43	      media[0].media_url,
    44	      "https://estate-4u.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/sample-home.jpg?ver=1",
    45	    );
    46	    assert.equal((normalized as any).image_filename, "sample-home.jpg");
    47	    assert.deepEqual((normalized as any).image_names, ["sample-home.jpg"]);
    48	  });
    49

    61	      },
    62	      "42",

FILE: frontend/lib/listingDisplay.ts

     1	/**
     2	 * Public vs privileged presentation for MLS listing pages (CREA / board display norms).
     3	 * TODO: set isPrivileged from agent/session when auth exists.
     4	 */
     5	
     6	import type { Property } from "@/lib/api";
     7	
     8	export type ListingDisplayOptions = {
     9	  isPrivileged: boolean;
    10	};
    11	
    12	/** QA override: NEXT_PUBLIC_LISTING_DISPLAY_PRIVILEGED=true shows full address and withheld pricing. */
    13	export function getListingIsPrivileged(): boolean {
    14	  if (
    15	    typeof process !== "undefined" &&
    16	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_LISTING_DISPLAY_PRIVILEGED === "true"
    17	  ) {
    18	    return true;
    19	  }
    20	  return false;
    21	}
    22	
    23	function parseListPrice(property: Property): number | null {
    24	  const raw = property.list_price ?? property.ListPrice;
    25	  if (raw === null || raw === undefined || raw === "") return null;
    26	  const n =
    27	    typeof raw === "string"
    28	      ? parseFloat(String(raw).replace(/[^0-9.-]+/g, ""))
    29	      : Number(raw);
    30	  if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return null;
    31	  if (n <= 0) return null;
    32	  return n;
    33	}
    34	
    35	function parseMoney(v: unknown): number | null {
    36	  if (v === null || v === undefined || v === "") return null;
    37	  const n = typeof v === "string" ? parseFloat(v) : Number(v);
    38	  return Number.isFinite(n) ? n : null;
    39	}
    40	
    41	/** True when a non-null list price exists (including 0). */
    42	export function hasListPrice(property: Property): boolean {
    43	  return parseListPrice(property) !== null;
    44	}
    45	
    46	/**
    47	 * Anonymous: neighbourhood / city / province only (no street).
    48	 * Privileged: street address when available.
    49	 */
    50	export function getDisplayAddress(
    51	  property: Property,
    52	  { isPrivileged }: ListingDisplayOptions,
    53	): string {
    54	  if (isPrivileged) {
    55	    const full =
    56	      property.unparsed_address ||
    57	      `${property.address || ""} ${property.city || ""}`.trim();
    58	    if (full) return full;
    59	  }
    60	
    61	  const city = property.city || property.City || "";
    62	  const region = property.city_region || property.CityRegion || "";
    63	  const prov =
    64	    property.state_or_province ||
    65	    property.StateOrProvince ||
    66	    property.province ||
    67	    "";
    68	
    69	  const area = [region, city].filter(Boolean).join(" · ");
    70	  if (area && prov) return `${area}, ${prov}`;
    71	  if (area) return area;
    72	  if (city && prov) return `${city}, ${prov}`;
    73	  if (city) return city;
    74	  return "Address not available";
    75	}
    76	
    77	/**
    78	 * Header/list price line. Anonymous + no list price: never show rent/lease as substitute.
    79	 */
    80	export function getDisplayPriceLabel(
    81	  property: Property,
    82	  { isPrivileged }: ListingDisplayOptions,
    83	): string {
    84	  const list = parseListPrice(property);
    85	  if (list !== null) {
    86	    return `$${list.toLocaleString("en-US")}`;
    87	  }
    88	  if (isPrivileged) {
    89	    const rent = parseMoney(property.total_actual_rent);
    90	    const lease = parseMoney(property.lease_amount);
    91	    if (rent !== null) return `$${rent.toLocaleString("en-US")}/month`;
    92	    if (lease !== null) return `$${lease.toLocaleString("en-US")}`;
    93	  }
    94	  return "Price on request";
    95	}
    96	
    97	export function getMortgageInitialPrice(
    98	  property: Property,
    99	  { isPrivileged }: ListingDisplayOptions,
   100	): number {
   101	  const list = parseListPrice(property);
   102	  if (list !== null && list > 0) return list;
   103	  if (isPrivileged) {
   104	    const rent = parseMoney(property.total_actual_rent);
   105	    if (rent !== null && rent > 0) return rent;
   106	    const lease = parseMoney(property.lease_amount);
   107	    if (lease !== null && lease > 0) return lease;
   108	  }
   109	  return 0;
   110	}
   111	
   112	/** Defaults for listing-page cash flow estimator (tax from annual; rent from lease fields when present). */
   113	export function getCashflowInitialsFromProperty(
   114	  property: Property,
   115	  { isPrivileged }: ListingDisplayOptions,
   116	): {
   117	  initialHomePrice: number;
   118	  initialMonthlyRent: number;
   119	  initialMonthlyPropertyTax: number;
   120	  initialAnnualMaintenance?: number;
   121	  initialOtherMonthly: number;
   122	} {
   123	  const home = getMortgageInitialPrice(property, { isPrivileged });
   124	  const taxAnnual =
   125	    parseMoney(
   126	      (property as { tax_annual_amount?: unknown }).tax_annual_amount ??
   127	        (property as { TaxAnnualAmount?: unknown }).TaxAnnualAmount,
   128	    ) ?? 0;
   129	  const monthlyTax = taxAnnual > 0 ? taxAnnual / 12 : 0;
   130	  const rent =
   131	    parseMoney(property.total_actual_rent) ??
   132	    parseMoney(property.lease_amount) ??
   133	    0;
   134	  const insurancePlaceholder = 0;
   135	  return {
   136	    initialHomePrice: home,
   137	    initialMonthlyRent: rent,
   138	    initialMonthlyPropertyTax: monthlyTax,
   139	    initialAnnualMaintenance: undefined,
   140	    initialOtherMonthly: insurancePlaceholder,
   141	  };
   142	}
   143	
   144	/** Monthly rent line for rental detail UI; null = hide row (withheld for anonymous). */
   145	export function getDisplayMonthlyRentLabel(
   146	  property: Property,
   147	  { isPrivileged }: ListingDisplayOptions,
   148	): string | null {
   149	  if (!isPrivileged && parseListPrice(property) === null) return null;
   150	  const rent = parseMoney(property.total_actual_rent);
   151	  if (rent === null) return null;
   152	  return `$${rent.toLocaleString("en-US")}/month`;
   153	}
   154	
   155	export function shouldShowMonthlyRentRow(
   156	  property: Property,
   157	  isPrivileged: boolean,
   158	): boolean {
   159	  if (parseMoney(property.total_actual_rent) === null) return false;
   160	  if (isPrivileged) return true;
   161	  return parseListPrice(property) !== null;
   162	}
   163	
   164	/** Property History table source column: no internal ListingKey for anonymous users. */
   165	export function getPropertyHistorySource(
   166	  property: Property,
   167	  { isPrivileged }: ListingDisplayOptions,
   168	): string {
   169	  if (isPrivileged) {
   170	    const lid = property.listing_id || (property as { ListingId?: string }).ListingId;
   171	    const lk = property.listing_key || property.ListingKey;
   172	    if (lid) return `MLS® # ${lid}`;
   173	    if (lk) return `MLS® # ${lk}`;
   174	  }
   175	  return "MLS® listing";
   176	}
   177	
   178	/** Consumer MLS® number for detail grids; optional second line for privileged. */
   179	export function getMlsNumberForDisplay(
   180	  property: Property,
   181	  { isPrivileged }: ListingDisplayOptions,
   182	): string | null {
   183	  const lid = property.listing_id || (property as { ListingId?: string }).ListingId;
   184	  const lk = property.listing_key || property.ListingKey;
   185	  if (isPrivileged) {
   186	    if (lid) return String(lid);
   187	    if (lk) return String(lk);
   188	    return null;
   189	  }
   190	  if (lid) return String(lid);
   191	  return null;
   192	}

================================================================
FILE: frontend/lib/propertyUtils.ts
================================================================
     1	/**
     2	 * Property Field Normalizer — Single Source of Truth
     3	 *
     4	 * The API returns properties with both `snake_case` and `PascalCase` field names.
     5	 * This module provides one canonical accessor for each field so that components
     6	 * never have to guess which casing to use.
     7	 *
     8	 * RULES:
     9	 *  - If you need a new property accessor, add it HERE — not inline.
    10	 *  - Always import from `@/lib/propertyUtils` — never access `property.city`
    11	 *    or `property.City` directly.
    12	 *  - The `Property` type comes from `@/lib/api`.
    13	 */
    14	
    15	import type { Property } from "@/lib/api";
    16	import { propertyCard } from "@/config/design-system";
    17	import { getMlsNumberForDisplay } from "@/lib/listingDisplay";
    18	
    19	export interface PropertyDetailItem {
    20	  label: string;
    21	  value: string;
    22	}
    23	
    24	export interface PropertyDetailSection {
    25	  id?: string;
    26	  kind?: "default" | "custom";
    27	  title: string;
    28	  items: PropertyDetailItem[];
    29	}
    30	
    31	export interface PropertyCustomDetailBlock {
    32	  id: string;
    33	  title: string;
    34	  order?: number;
    35	  items: PropertyDetailItem[];
    36	}
    37	
    38	export interface PropertyDetailBlockLayoutItem {
    39	  id: string;
    40	  kind: "default" | "custom";
    41	  order: number;
    42	  visible: boolean;
    43	}
    44	
    45	export interface ListingActionButton {
    46	  id: string;
    47	  label: string;
    48	  href: string;
    49	  order: number;
    50	  requiresPhoneVerification: boolean;
    51	}
    52	
    53	/* ──────────────────────────── Identity ──────────────────────────── */
    54	// this is the single source of truth for the unique key of a property, which is used for things like compare and quick view interactions. It falls back to a generated key based on city and price if no explicit listing key is available, to ensure that every property can be uniquely identified in the UI. This is important because some of our data sources (especially pre-construction) may not have consistent unique identifiers, so we need a robust way to generate them when missing.
    55	export const getPropertyKey = (property: Property): string =>
    56	  property.listing_key ||
    57	  property.PropertyKey ||
    58	  `property-${property.city || property.City || "unknown"}-${property.ListPrice || property.list_price || "0"
    59	  }`;
    60	
    61	/* ──────────────────────────── Location ──────────────────────────── */
    62	
    63	export const getCity = (property: Property): string =>
    64	  property.city || property.City || "Unknown City";
    65	
    66	export const getProvince = (property: Property): string =>
    67	  property.province ||
    68	  property.state_or_province ||
    69	  property.StateOrProvince ||
    70	  "";
    71	
    72	export const getPostalCode = (property: Property): string =>
    73	  property.postal_code || property.PostalCode || "";
    74	
    75	export const getAddress = (property: Property): string | null =>
    76	  property.unparsed_address || property.address || null;
    77	
    78	export const getFullAddress = (property: Property): string => {
    79	  const parts = [
    80	    getAddress(property),
    81	    getCity(property),
    82	    getProvince(property),
    83	    getPostalCode(property),
    84	  ].filter(Boolean);
    85	  return parts.join(", ");
    86	};
    87	
    88	export const getLatitude = (property: Property): number | null => {
    89	  const val = property.latitude || property.Latitude;
    90	  if (!val) return null;
    91	  const num = typeof val === "string" ? parseFloat(val) : val;
    92	  return Number.isFinite(num) ? num : null;
    93	};
    94	
    95	export const getLongitude = (property: Property): number | null => {
    96	  const val = property.longitude || property.Longitude;
    97	  if (!val) return null;
    98	  const num = typeof val === "string" ? parseFloat(val) : val;
    99	  return Number.isFinite(num) ? num : null;
   100	};
   101	
   102	/* ──────────────────────────── Pricing ──────────────────────────── */
   103	
   104	export const getPrice = (property: Property): number => {
   105	  const possible =
   106	    (property as any).list_price ??
   107	    property.ListPrice ??
   108	    (property as any).ListPriceNumeric ??
   109	    0;
   110	  if (typeof possible === "string") {
   111	    const parsed = parseFloat(possible.replace(/[^0-9.-]+/g, ""));
   112	    return Number.isFinite(parsed) ? parsed : 0;
   113	  }
   114	  return typeof possible === "number" ? possible : 0;
   115	};
   116	
   117	export const formatPrice = (price: number): string =>
   118	  price > 0
   119	    ? new Intl.NumberFormat(propertyCard.currency.locale, {
   120	      style: "currency",
   121	      currency: propertyCard.currency.code,
   122	      minimumFractionDigits: 0,
   123	      maximumFractionDigits: 0,
   124	    }).format(price)
   125	    : propertyCard.fallbackText.noPrice;
   126	
   127	/* ──────────────────────────── Classification ──────────────────────────── */
   128

   130	export const getPropertyType = (property: Property): string =>
   131	  property.property_sub_type ||
   132	  property.PropertySubType ||
   133	  property.PropertyType ||
   134	  "Property";

   137	  property.standard_status || property.StandardStatus || "For Sale";

   141	export const getBedrooms = (property: Property): number => {
   142	  const val = property.bedrooms_total ?? property.BedroomsTotal ?? 0;
   143	  return typeof val === "string" ? parseFloat(val) || 0 : (val as number);
   144	};
   145	
   146	export const getBathrooms = (property: Property): number => {
   147	  const val =
   148	    property.bathrooms_total_integer ?? property.BathroomsTotalInteger ?? 0;
   149	  return typeof val === "string" ? parseFloat(val) || 0 : (val as number);
   150	};
   151	
   152	export const getSqft = (property: Property): number | null => {
   153	  const val =
   154	    property.building_area_total ??
   155	    (property as any).LivingArea ??
   156	    (property as any).LivingAreaMinimum ??
   157	    null;
   158	  if (!val) return null;
   159	  const num = typeof val === "string" ? parseFloat(val) : val;
   160	  return Number.isFinite(num) && num > 0 ? num : null;
   161	};
   162	
   163	export const getYearBuilt = (property: Property): number | null => {
   164	  const val = property.year_built ?? (property as any).YearBuilt ?? null;
   165	  if (!val) return null;
   166	  const num = typeof val === "string" ? parseInt(val, 10) : val;
   167	  return Number.isFinite(num) && num > 1800 ? num : null;
   168	};

   171	  property.parking_total ?? (property as any).GarageSpaces ?? null;

   173	/* ──────────────────────────── Media ──────────────────────────── */
   174	
   175	const MEDIA_URL_KEYS = [
   176	  "url",
   177	  "media_url",
   178	  "MediaURL",
   179	  "MediaUrl",
   180	  "src",
   181	  "thumbnail",
   182	  "thumbnailUrl",
   183	  "thumbnail_url",
   184	  "featured_image_url",
   185	  "primary_image_url",
   186	  "image_url",
   187	  "ImageURL",
   188	  "imageUrl",
   189	] as const;
   190	
   191	export const getThumbnail = (property: Property): string | null => {
   192	  const candidates = [
   193	    (property as any).photos,
   194	    property.Photos,
   195	    property.media,
   196	    property.Media,
   197	    (property as any).images,
   198	    (property as any).Images,
   199	    (property as any).featured_image_url,
   200	    (property as any).primary_image_url,
   201	    (property as any).image_url,
   202	    (property as any).thumbnail_url,
   203	  ];
   204	
   205	  for (const field of candidates) {
   206	    if (!field) continue;
   207	
   208	    if (Array.isArray(field) && field.length > 0) {
   209	      const first = field[0];
   210	      if (typeof first === "string" && first.trim()) return first;
   211	      if (typeof first === "object" && first !== null) {
   212	        for (const k of MEDIA_URL_KEYS) {
   213	          if (first[k]) return first[k];
   214	        }
   215	      }
   216	    }
   217	
   218	    if (typeof field === "object" && !Array.isArray(field)) {
   219	      for (const k of MEDIA_URL_KEYS) {
   220	        if ((field as any)[k]) return (field as any)[k];
   221	      }
   222	    }
   223	
   224	    if (typeof field === "string" && field.trim()) return field;
   225	  }
   226	  return null;
   227	};
   228	
   229	export const getPhotos = (property: Property): string[] => {
   230	  const candidates = [
   231	    (property as any).photos,
   232	    property.Photos,
   233	    property.media,
   234	    property.Media,
   235	    (property as any).images,
   236	    (property as any).Images,
   237	    (property as any).featured_image_url,
   238	    (property as any).primary_image_url,
   239	    (property as any).image_url,
   240	    (property as any).thumbnail_url,
   241	  ];
   242	
   243	  const allPhotos: string[] = [];
   244	
   245	  for (const field of candidates) {
   246	    if (!field) continue;
   247	
   248	    if (Array.isArray(field) && field.length > 0) {
   249	      for (const item of field) {
   250	        if (typeof item === "string" && item.trim()) {
   251	          allPhotos.push(item);
   252	        } else if (typeof item === "object" && item !== null) {
   253	          for (const k of MEDIA_URL_KEYS) {
   254	            if ((item as any)[k]) {
   255	              allPhotos.push((item as any)[k]);
   256	              break;
   257	            }
   258	          }
   259	        }
   260	      }
   261	    } else if (typeof field === "object") {
   262	      for (const k of MEDIA_URL_KEYS) {
   263	        if ((field as any)[k]) {
   264	          allPhotos.push((field as any)[k]);
   265	          break;
   266	        }
   267	      }
   268	    } else if (typeof field === "string" && field.trim()) {
   269	      allPhotos.push(field);
   270	    }
   271	
   272	    if (allPhotos.length > 0) break;
   273	  }
   274	
   275	  // Deduplicate
   276	  return allPhotos.filter((item, index) => allPhotos.indexOf(item) === index);
   277	};
   278	
   279	export const getPhotosCount = (property: Property): number => {
   280	  const photos = getPhotos(property);
   281	  return photos.length || (property as any).photos_count || 0;
   282	};

   285	
   286	export const getListingDate = (property: Property): string => {
   287	  const fields = [
   288	    (property as any).listing_date,
   289	    (property as any).ListingDate,
   290	    (property as any).list_date,
   291	    (property as any).ListDate,
   292	    (property as any).modification_timestamp,
   293	    property.ModificationTimestamp,
   294	    (property as any).updated_at,
   295	    (property as any).created_at,
   296	    (property as any).CreatedAt,
   297	  ];
   298	
   299	  for (const field of fields) {
   300	    if (field) {
   301	      const date = new Date(field);
   302	      if (!isNaN(date.getTime())) {
   303	        return date.toLocaleDateString(propertyCard.currency.locale, {
   304	          month: "short",
   305	          day: "numeric",
   306	          year: "numeric",
   307	        });
   308	      }
   309	    }
   310	  }
   311	  return "Recently listed";
   312	};

   317	  null;

   321	const HTML_TAG_RE = /<[^>]*>/g;
   322	
   323	const normalizeRichText = (value: unknown): string => {
   324	  if (value == null) return "";
   325	  return String(value)
   326	    .replace(HTML_TAG_RE, " ")
   327	    .replace(/&nbsp;/gi, " ")
   328	    .replace(/\s+/g, " ")
   329	    .trim();
   330	};
   331	
   332	export const getDescription = (property: Property): string =>
   333	  normalizeRichText(
   334	    property.property_description ||
   335	      property.PropertyDescription ||
   336	      property.public_remarks ||
   337	      property.PublicRemarks ||
   338	      "",
   339	  );

   341	export const getListingUrl = (property: Property): string | null =>
   342	  property.listing_url || null;
   343	
   344	/** Canadian postal FSA (first 3 alphanumeric chars, spaces removed). */
   345	export function postalToFsa(
   346	  postal: string | null | undefined,
   347	): string | null {
   348	  if (!postal || typeof postal !== "string") return null;
   349	  const alnum = postal.replace(/[^A-Za-z0-9]/g, "").toUpperCase();
   350	  if (alnum.length < 3) return null;
   351	  return alnum.slice(0, 3);
   352	}

   354	/* ──────────────────────────── Navigation ──────────────────────────── */
   355	
   356	/**
   357	 * Checks if the property is a rental/lease based on various possible API fields.
   358	 */
   359	export const isRental = (property: Property): boolean => {
   360	  const type = (property.PropertyType || "").toLowerCase();
   361	  const subType = (
   362	    property.PropertySubType ||
   363	    property.property_sub_type ||
   364	    ""
   365	  ).toLowerCase();
   366	  const status = (
   367	    property.standard_status ||
   368	    property.StandardStatus ||
   369	    ""
   370	  ).toLowerCase();
   371	
   372	  return (
   373	    type.includes("lease") ||
   374	    type.includes("rental") ||
   375	    subType.includes("lease") ||
   376	    subType.includes("rental") ||
   377	    status.includes("lease") ||
   378	    status.includes("rent") ||
   379	    !!property.lease_amount ||
   380	    !!property.total_actual_rent
   381	  );
   382	};
   383	
   384	const isPreConstruction = (property: Property): boolean => {
   385	  const type = String(
   386	    property.property_sub_type || property.PropertySubType || property.PropertyType || "",
   387	  ).toLowerCase();
   388	  const status = String(
   389	    property.standard_status || property.StandardStatus || "",
   390	  ).toLowerCase();
   391	  const city = String(property.city || property.City || "").toLowerCase();
   392	  const key = String(property.listing_key || property.PropertyKey || "").toLowerCase();
   393	  const rawKey = String(property.listing_key || property.PropertyKey || "").trim();
   394	
   395	  return (
   396	    key.startsWith("precon_") ||
   397	    type.includes("pre-construction") ||
   398	    type.includes("pre construction") ||
   399	    status.includes("pre-construction") ||
   400	    status.includes("pre construction") ||
   401	    city === "pre-construction" ||
   402	    // WP precon ids are numeric; normalize them into precon_<id> routes.
   403	    (/^\d+$/.test(rawKey) &&
   404	      (type.includes("pre") || status.includes("pre") || city.includes("pre")))
   405	  );
   406	};
   407	
   408	/**
   409	 * Returns the canonical detail page URL for a property.
   410	 * Canocial means it will always return a URL in the format of `/listing/${key}` or `/listing/rental/${key}` or `/estate-listing/${key}` for estates, regardless of the original API fields available. This ensures that all components can link to property details consistently without worrying about the underlying data structure.
   411	 */
   412	export const getDetailUrl = (property: Property): string => {
   413	  let key = getPropertyKey(property);
   414	  const rental = isRental(property);
   415	  const isEstate = String(key).startsWith("estate_");
   416	  // Estate listings have their own detail pipeline. Do not re-prefix as precon.
   417	  if (isEstate) return `/estate-listing/${key}`;
   418	  if (isPreConstruction(property) && !String(key).startsWith("precon_")) {
   419	    key = `precon_${key}`;
   420	  }
   421	  return rental ? `/listing/rental/${key}` : `/listing/${key}`;
   422	};
   423	
   424	const toValue = (value: unknown): string | null => {
   425	  if (value === null || value === undefined) return null;
   426	  if (typeof value === "string") {
   427	    const trimmed = value.trim();
   428	    return trimmed.length > 0 ? trimmed : null;
   429	  }
   430	  if (typeof value === "number") {
   431	    return Number.isFinite(value) ? String(value) : null;
   432	  }
   433	  if (typeof value === "boolean") {
   434	    return value ? "Yes" : "No";
   435	  }
   436	  return null;
   437	};
   438	
   439	const getRaw = (property: Property, ...keys: string[]): unknown => {
   440	  for (const key of keys) {
   441	    const value = (property as Record<string, unknown>)[key];
   442	    if (
   443	      value !== null &&
   444	      value !== undefined &&
   445	      !(typeof value === "string" && value.trim() === "")
   446	    ) {
   447	      return value;
   448	    }
   449	  }
   450	  return null;
   451	};
   452	
   453	const formatNumber = (value: unknown): string | null => {
   454	  const raw = toValue(value);
   455	  if (!raw) return null;
   456	  const parsed = Number(raw.replace(/,/g, ""));
   457	  if (!Number.isFinite(parsed)) return raw;
   458	  return parsed.toLocaleString("en-US");
   459	};
   460	
   461	const formatCurrency = (value: unknown): string | null => {
   462	  const raw = toValue(value);
   463	  if (!raw) return null;
   464	  const parsed = Number(raw.replace(/[^0-9.-]+/g, ""));
   465	  if (!Number.isFinite(parsed)) return raw;
   466	  return `$${parsed.toLocaleString("en-US", { maximumFractionDigits: 0 })}`;
   467	};
   468	
   469	const formatList = (value: unknown): string | null => {
   470	  if (!Array.isArray(value)) return toValue(value);
   471	  const compact = value
   472	    .map((entry) => {
   473	      if (entry && typeof entry === "object") {
   474	        const typed = entry as Record<string, unknown>;
   475	        return toValue(typed.name ?? typed.label ?? typed.value);
   476	      }
   477	      return toValue(entry);
   478	    })
   479	    .filter((entry): entry is string => Boolean(entry));
   480	  return compact.length ? compact.join(", ") : null;
   481	};
   482	
   483	const parseJsonMap = (value: unknown): Record<string, unknown> => {
   484	  if (value && typeof value === "object" && !Array.isArray(value)) {
   485	    return value as Record<string, unknown>;
   486	  }
   487	  if (typeof value !== "string") return {};
   488	  try {
   489	    const parsed = JSON.parse(value);
   490	    return parsed && typeof parsed === "object" && !Array.isArray(parsed)
   491	      ? (parsed as Record<string, unknown>)
   492	      : {};
   493	  } catch {
   494	    return {};
   495	  }
   496	};
   497	
   498	const getTaxonomyList = (
   499	  property: Property,
   500	  ...keys: string[]
   501	): string | null => {
   502	  const direct = formatList(getRaw(property, ...keys));
   503	  if (direct) return direct;
   504	
   505	  const wpTerms = parseJsonMap((property as Record<string, unknown>).wp_terms_json);
   506	  for (const key of keys) {
   507	    const value = formatList(wpTerms[key]);
   508	    if (value) return value;
   509	  }
   510	  return null;
   511	};
   512	
   513	const normalizeRangeText = (value: unknown): string | null => {
   514	  const text = toValue(value);
   515	  if (!text) return null;
   516	  if (!/^\d+(\.\d+)?\s*[-–]\s*\d+(\.\d+)?$/.test(text)) return null;
   517	  return text.replace(/[–]/g, "-").replace(/\s+/g, "");
   518	};
   519	
   520	const getWpMetaField = (property: Property, key: string): string | null => {
   521	  const rawMeta = (property as Record<string, unknown>).wp_meta_json;
   522	  if (rawMeta && typeof rawMeta === "object" && !Array.isArray(rawMeta)) {
   523	    const value = (rawMeta as Record<string, unknown>)[key];
   524	    return toValue(value);
   525	  }
   526	  if (typeof rawMeta === "string") {
   527	    try {
   528	      const parsed = JSON.parse(rawMeta);
   529	      if (parsed && typeof parsed === "object" && !Array.isArray(parsed)) {
   530	        return toValue((parsed as Record<string, unknown>)[key]);
   531	      }
   532	    } catch {
   533	      return null;
   534	    }
   535	  }
   536	  return null;
   537	};
   538	
   539	export const getTaxAnnualAmount = (property: Property): string | null => {
   540	  const raw = getRaw(property, "tax_annual_amount", "TaxAnnualAmount");
   541	  return formatCurrency(raw);
   542	};
   543	
   544	export const getParkingSummary = (property: Property): string | null => {
   545	  const total = formatNumber(getRaw(property, "parking_total", "ParkingTotal"));
   546	  const features = formatList(
   547	    getRaw(property, "parking_features", "ParkingFeatures"),
   548	  );
   549	  if (total && features) return `${total} (${features})`;
   550	  return total || features || null;
   551	};
   552	
   553	export const getLotSizeSummary = (property: Property): string | null => {
   554	  const dimensions = toValue(
   555	    getRaw(
   556	      property,
   557	      "lot_size_dimensions",
   558	      "LotSizeDimensions",
   559	      "lot_size",
   560	      "LotSize",
   561	    ),
   562	  );
   563	  if (dimensions) return dimensions;
   564	  const areaRaw = toValue(
   565	    getRaw(property, "lot_size_area", "LotSizeArea", "land_area", "LandArea"),
   566	  );
   567	  if (!areaRaw) return null;
   568	  const areaNum = Number(String(areaRaw).replace(/,/g, ""));
   569	  const area = Number.isFinite(areaNum) ? areaNum.toLocaleString("en-US") : areaRaw;
   570	  return `${area} sq ft`;
   571	};
   572	
   573	export const getPropertySizeSummary = (property: Property): string | null => {
   574	  const sizeValue = toValue(getRaw(property, "lot_size", "LotSize"));
   575	  if (!sizeValue) return null;
   576	  const postfix =
   577	    toValue(getRaw(property, "size_postfix", "SizePostfix")) || "sq ft";
   578	  return `${sizeValue} ${postfix}`.trim();
   579	};
   580	
   581	/** Prefer living area min–max range when both exist (matches DDF LivingAreaMinimum / Maximum). */
   582	export const getLivingAreaSummary = (property: Property): string => {
   583	  const minStr = toValue(
   584	    getRaw(property, "living_area_minimum", "LivingAreaMinimum"),
   585	  );
   586	  const maxStr = toValue(
   587	    getRaw(property, "living_area_maximum", "LivingAreaMaximum"),
   588	  );
   589	  const minN = minStr ? Number(String(minStr).replace(/,/g, "")) : NaN;
   590	  const maxN = maxStr ? Number(String(maxStr).replace(/,/g, "")) : NaN;
   591	  if (Number.isFinite(minN) && Number.isFinite(maxN)) {
   592	    if (minN === maxN) return `${minN.toLocaleString("en-US")} sq ft`;
   593	    return `${minN.toLocaleString("en-US")} - ${maxN.toLocaleString("en-US")} sq ft`;
   594	  }
   595	  const singleRaw =
   596	    toValue(getRaw(property, "building_area_total", "BuildingAreaTotal")) ||
   597	    toValue(getRaw(property, "living_area", "LivingArea")) ||
   598	    (Number.isFinite(minN) ? minN.toLocaleString("en-US") : "");
   599	  if (!singleRaw) return "";
   600	  const singleNum = Number(String(singleRaw).replace(/,/g, ""));
   601	  const single = Number.isFinite(singleNum) ? singleNum.toLocaleString("en-US") : singleRaw;
   602	  return `${single} sq ft`;
   603	};
   604	
   605	/** Quick facts / stats: total baths plus partial count when present. */
   606	export const getBathroomDisplayLabel = (property: Property): string | null => {
   607	  const totalRaw =
   608	    property.bathrooms_total_integer ?? property.BathroomsTotalInteger ?? null;
   609	  const directRange = normalizeRangeText(totalRaw);
   610	  if (directRange) {
   611	    return directRange;
   612	  }
   613	  const maxFromMeta = Number(getWpMetaField(property, "max_bathrooms"));
   614	  const partialRaw =
   615	    property.bathrooms_partial ?? property.BathroomsPartial ?? null;
   616	  const t =
   617	    totalRaw === null || totalRaw === ""
   618	      ? NaN
   619	      : typeof totalRaw === "string"
   620	        ? parseInt(totalRaw, 10)
   621	        : Number(totalRaw);
   622	  const p =
   623	    partialRaw === null || partialRaw === ""
   624	      ? NaN
   625	      : typeof partialRaw === "string"
   626	        ? parseInt(partialRaw, 10)
   627	        : Number(partialRaw);
   628	  if (!Number.isFinite(t) || t <= 0) return null;
   629	  if (Number.isFinite(maxFromMeta) && maxFromMeta > t) {
   630	    return `${t}-${maxFromMeta}`;
   631	  }
   632	  if (Number.isFinite(p) && p > 0) {
   633	    return `${t} (${p} partial)`;
   634	  }
   635	  return String(t);
   636	};
   637	
   638	/** Quick facts / stats: bedrooms count, preserving ranges (e.g. "3-5"). */
   639	export const getBedroomDisplayLabel = (property: Property): string | null => {
   640	  const minRaw = getRaw(property, "bedrooms_total", "BedroomsTotal");
   641	  const maxRaw = getRaw(property, "max_bedrooms", "MaxBedrooms");
   642	
   643	  const directRange = normalizeRangeText(minRaw);
   644	  if (directRange) {
   645	    return directRange;
   646	  }
   647	
   648	  const minText = toValue(minRaw);
   649	  const minNum = Number(minText);
   650	  const maxNum = Number(toValue(maxRaw));
   651	  const hasMin = Number.isFinite(minNum) && minNum > 0;
   652	  const hasMax = Number.isFinite(maxNum) && maxNum > 0;
   653	
   654	  if (hasMin && hasMax && maxNum > minNum) {
   655	    return `${minNum}-${maxNum}`;
   656	  }
   657	  if (hasMin) return String(minNum);
   658	  if (hasMax) return String(maxNum);
   659	  return minText || null;
   660	};
   661	
   662	/** Quick facts / stats: garages count, preserving ranges (e.g. "1-3"). */
   663	export const getGarageDisplayLabel = (property: Property): string | null => {
   664	  const minRaw = getRaw(property, "garages", "Garages");
   665	  const directRange = normalizeRangeText(minRaw);
   666	  if (directRange) return directRange;
   667	
   668	  const minText = toValue(minRaw);
   669	  const minNum = Number(minText);
   670	  const maxFromMeta = Number(getWpMetaField(property, "max_garages"));
   671	  const hasMin = Number.isFinite(minNum) && minNum > 0;
   672	  const hasMax = Number.isFinite(maxFromMeta) && maxFromMeta > 0;
   673	
   674	  if (hasMin && hasMax && maxFromMeta > minNum) return `${minNum}-${maxFromMeta}`;
   675	  if (hasMin) return String(minNum);
   676	  if (hasMax) return String(maxFromMeta);
   677	  return minText || null;
   678	};

   680	/** Annual tax amount with tax year when available (e.g. MLS TaxAnnualAmount + TaxYear). */
   681	export const getAnnualTaxDisplayWithYear = (property: Property): string | null => {
   682	  const amt = getTaxAnnualAmount(property);
   683	  const year = toValue(getRaw(property, "tax_year", "TaxYear"));
   684	  if (amt && year) return `${amt} (${year})`;
   685	  if (amt) return amt;
   686	  if (year) return `Tax year ${year}`;
   687	  return null;
   688	};

   690	/** Lat/lng as plain text for listing detail (six decimal places). */
   691	export const getCoordinatesLabel = (property: Property): string | null => {
   692	  const lat = getLatitude(property);
   693	  const lon = getLongitude(property);
   694	  if (lat === null || lon === null) return null;
   695	  return `${lat.toFixed(6)}, ${lon.toFixed(6)}`;
   696	};
   697	
   698	const EXTERNAL_MEDIA_CATEGORY =
   699	  /video tour|virtual tour|additional pictures|unbranded virtual/i;
   700	
   701	const DDFCDN_PHOTO =
   702	  /^https:\/\/ddfcdn\.realtor\.ca\/.*\.(jpe?g|png|webp)(\?|$)/i;
   703	
   704	/**
   705	 * Non-photo MLS media links (virtual tour site, extra photo galleries, Matterport, etc.).
   706	 */
   707	export const getListingExternalMediaLinks = (
   708	  property: Property,
   709	): { label: string; url: string }[] => {
   710	  const rows = (property.media || property.Media || []) as unknown as Array<
   711	    Record<string, unknown>
   712	  >;
   713	  const seen = new Set<string>();
   714	  const out: { label: string; url: string }[] = [];
   715	
   716	  for (const row of rows) {
   717	    const url = String(row.media_url ?? row.MediaURL ?? "").trim();
   718	    if (!/^https?:\/\//i.test(url) || seen.has(url)) continue;
   719	
   720	    const cat = String(row.media_category ?? row.MediaCategory ?? "").trim();
   721	    if (DDFCDN_PHOTO.test(url) && /property photo|^photo$/i.test(cat)) continue;
   722	
   723	    const looksExternal =
   724	      EXTERNAL_MEDIA_CATEGORY.test(cat) ||
   725	      /insideottawamedia|matterport|my3d|tour\.|vimeo\.com|youtu\.be|youtube\.com/i.test(
   726	        url,
   727	      );
   728	    if (!looksExternal) continue;
   729	
   730	    seen.add(url);
   731	    let label = cat || "External media";
   732	    if (/video tour/i.test(cat)) label = "Video tour";
   733	    else if (/additional pictures/i.test(cat)) label = "More photos (external site)";
   734	    else if (/unbranded virtual/i.test(cat)) label = "Virtual tour";
   735	    out.push({ label, url });
   736	  }
   737	  return out;
   738	};
   739	
   740	const toDetailItem = (
   741	  label: string,
   742	  value: string | null,
   743	): PropertyDetailItem | null => {
   744	  if (!value) return null;
   745	  const trimmed = value.trim();
   746	  if (!trimmed || trimmed.toLowerCase() === "n/a" || trimmed.toLowerCase() === "null") {
   747	    return null;
   748	  }
   749	  return { label, value: trimmed };
   750	};
   751	
   752	const DEFAULT_DETAIL_BLOCK_IDS = [
   753	  "financial_information",
   754	  "building_facts",
   755	  "location_access",
   756	  "lot_land",
   757	  "construction_systems",
   758	  "utilities_services",
   759	  "parking_structure",
   760	  "listing_details",
   761	] as const;
   762	
   763	function parseJsonArray(value: unknown): unknown[] {
   764	  if (Array.isArray(value)) return value;
   765	  if (typeof value !== "string") return [];
   766	  const text = value.trim();
   767	  if (!text) return [];
   768	  try {
   769	    const parsed = JSON.parse(text);
   770	    return Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed : [];
   771	  } catch {
   772	    return [];
   773	  }
   774	}
   775	
   776	export function getDefaultPropertyDetailBlockLayout(): PropertyDetailBlockLayoutItem[] {
   777	  return DEFAULT_DETAIL_BLOCK_IDS.map((id, index) => ({
   778	    id,
   779	    kind: "default",
   780	    order: index,
   781	    visible: true,
   782	  }));
   783	}
   784	
   785	export function normalizePropertyCustomDetailBlocks(
   786	  value: unknown,
   787	): PropertyCustomDetailBlock[] {
   788	  const rows = parseJsonArray(value);
   789	  return rows
   790	    .map((block, blockIndex): PropertyCustomDetailBlock | null => {
   791	      if (!block || typeof block !== "object") return null;
   792	      const typed = block as Record<string, unknown>;
   793	      const id = String(typed.id || `custom_detail_block_${blockIndex + 1}`).trim();
   794	      const title = String(typed.title || "").trim();
   795	      const items = parseJsonArray(typed.items)
   796	        .map((item): PropertyDetailItem | null => {
   797	          if (!item || typeof item !== "object") return null;
   798	          const row = item as Record<string, unknown>;
   799	          return toDetailItem(
   800	            String(row.label || ""),
   801	            String(row.value ?? ""),
   802	          );
   803	        })
   804	        .filter((item): item is PropertyDetailItem => Boolean(item));
   805	      if (!id || !title || items.length === 0) return null;
   806	      const order =
   807	        typeof typed.order === "number"
   808	          ? typed.order
   809	          : Number.parseInt(String(typed.order ?? blockIndex), 10);
   810	      return {
   811	        id,
   812	        title,
   813	        order: Number.isFinite(order) ? order : blockIndex,
   814	        items,
   815	      };
   816	    })
   817	    .filter((block): block is PropertyCustomDetailBlock => Boolean(block))
   818	    .sort((a, b) => (a.order ?? 0) - (b.order ?? 0));
   819	}
   820	
   821	export function normalizePropertyDetailBlockLayout(
   822	  value: unknown,
   823	): PropertyDetailBlockLayoutItem[] {
   824	  const rows = parseJsonArray(value);
   825	  return rows
   826	    .map((item, index): PropertyDetailBlockLayoutItem | null => {
   827	      if (!item || typeof item !== "object") return null;
   828	      const typed = item as Record<string, unknown>;
   829	      const id = String(typed.id || "").trim();
   830	      if (!id) return null;
   831	      const kind = typed.kind === "custom" ? "custom" : "default";
   832	      const order =
   833	        typeof typed.order === "number"
   834	          ? typed.order
   835	          : Number.parseInt(String(typed.order ?? index), 10);
   836	      return {
   837	        id,
   838	        kind,
   839	        order: Number.isFinite(order) ? order : index,
   840	        visible: typed.visible !== false,
   841	      };
   842	    })
   843	    .filter((item): item is PropertyDetailBlockLayoutItem => Boolean(item))
   844	    .sort((a, b) => a.order - b.order);
   845	}
   846	
   847	export function normalizeListingActionButtons(value: unknown): ListingActionButton[] {
   848	  const rows = parseJsonArray(value);
   849	  return rows
   850	    .map((item, index): ListingActionButton | null => {
   851	      if (!item || typeof item !== "object") return null;
   852	      const typed = item as Record<string, unknown>;
   853	      const id = String(typed.id || `listing-button-${index + 1}`).trim();
   854	      const label = String(typed.label || "").trim();
   855	      const href = String(typed.href || "").trim();
   856	      if (!id || !label || !/^https?:\/\//i.test(href)) return null;
   857	      const order =
   858	        typeof typed.order === "number"
   859	          ? typed.order
   860	          : Number.parseInt(String(typed.order ?? index), 10);
   861	      const requiresPhoneVerification =
   862	        typeof typed.requires_phone_verification === "boolean"
   863	          ? typed.requires_phone_verification
   864	          : ["1", "true", "yes", "y", "on"].includes(
   865	              String(typed.requires_phone_verification ?? "")
   866	                .trim()
   867	                .toLowerCase(),
   868	            );
   869	      return {
   870	        id,
   871	        label,
   872	        href,
   873	        order: Number.isFinite(order) ? order : index,
   874	        requiresPhoneVerification,
   875	      };
   876	    })
   877	    .filter((button): button is ListingActionButton => Boolean(button))
   878	    .sort((a, b) => a.order - b.order);
   879	}

   881	export type PropertyDetailSectionsOptions = {
