   885	export const getPropertyDetailSections = (
   886	  property: Property,
   887	  core: { price: string; type: string; livingArea: string },
   888	  options: PropertyDetailSectionsOptions = {},
   889	): PropertyDetailSection[] => {
   890	  const isPrivileged = options.isPrivileged ?? false;
   891	  const sections: PropertyDetailSection[] = [];
   892	
   893	  const pushSection = (
   894	    id: string,
   895	    title: string,
   896	    items: Array<PropertyDetailItem | null>,
   897	  ) => {
   898	    const filtered = items.filter((item): item is PropertyDetailItem => Boolean(item));
   899	    if (filtered.length > 0) sections.push({ id, kind: "default", title, items: filtered });
   900	  };
   901	
   902	  const mlsDisplay = getMlsNumberForDisplay(property, { isPrivileged });
   903	
   904	  pushSection("financial_information", "Financial Information", [
   905	    toDetailItem("List Price", core.price),
   906	    toDetailItem(
   907	      "Status",
   908	      toValue(getRaw(property, "standard_status", "StandardStatus")),
   909	    ),
   910	    toDetailItem("MLS® #", mlsDisplay),
   911	    toDetailItem("Annual Taxes", getTaxAnnualAmount(property)),
   912	    toDetailItem("Tax Year", toValue(getRaw(property, "tax_year", "TaxYear"))),
   913	    toDetailItem(
   914	      "Common Interest",
   915	      toValue(getRaw(property, "common_interest", "CommonInterest")),
   916	    ),
   917	  ]);
   918	
   919	  const partialBathCount = Number(
   920	    toValue(getRaw(property, "bathrooms_partial", "BathroomsPartial")),
   921	  );
   922	
   923	  pushSection("building_facts", "Building Facts", [
   924	    toDetailItem("Property Type", core.type),
   925	    toDetailItem("Property Size", getPropertySizeSummary(property) || core.livingArea),
   926	    toDetailItem(
   927	      "Year Built",
   928	      toValue(getRaw(property, "year_built", "YearBuilt")),
   929	    ),
   930	    toDetailItem(
   931	      "Stories",
   932	      toValue(getRaw(property, "stories", "Stories")),
   933	    ),
   934	    toDetailItem(
   935	      "Bedrooms Above Grade",
   936	      toValue(getRaw(property, "bedrooms_above_grade", "BedroomsAboveGrade")),
   937	    ),
   938	    Number.isFinite(partialBathCount) && partialBathCount > 0
   939	      ? toDetailItem("Partial bathrooms", String(partialBathCount))
   940	      : null,
   941	    toDetailItem("Developer", toValue(getRaw(property, "developer", "Developer"))),
   942	    toDetailItem(
   943	      "Occupancy Year",
   944	      toValue(getRaw(property, "occupancy_year", "OccupancyYear")),
   945	    ),
   946	    toDetailItem("Features", getTaxonomyList(property, "features", "property_feature")),
   947	  ]);
   948	
   949	  pushSection("location_access", "Location & access", [
   950	    toDetailItem("Directions", toValue(getRaw(property, "directions", "Directions"))),
   951	    toDetailItem("Coordinates", getCoordinatesLabel(property)),
   952	  ]);
   953	
   954	  pushSection("lot_land", "Lot & Land", [
   955	    toDetailItem(
   956	      "Frontage",
   957	      toValue(
   958	        getRaw(
   959	          property,
   960	          "frontage_length_numeric",
   961	          "FrontageLengthNumeric",
   962	          "frontage_length",
   963	          "FrontageLength",
   964	        ),
   965	      ),
   966	    ),
   967	    toDetailItem(
   968	      "Lot Features",
   969	      formatList(getRaw(property, "lot_features", "LotFeatures")),
   970	    ),
   971	    toDetailItem(
   972	      "Pool Features",
   973	      formatList(getRaw(property, "pool_features", "PoolFeatures")),
   974	    ),
   975	  ]);
   976	
   977	  pushSection("construction_systems", "Construction & Systems", [
   978	    toDetailItem("Heating", formatList(getRaw(property, "heating", "Heating"))),
   979	    toDetailItem("Cooling", formatList(getRaw(property, "cooling", "Cooling"))),
   980	    toDetailItem("Basement", formatList(getRaw(property, "basement", "Basement"))),
   981	    toDetailItem(
   982	      "Foundation",
   983	      formatList(getRaw(property, "foundation_details", "FoundationDetails")),
   984	    ),
   985	    toDetailItem("Roof", formatList(getRaw(property, "roof", "Roof"))),
   986	    toDetailItem(
   987	      "Exterior",
   988	      formatList(getRaw(property, "exterior_features", "ExteriorFeatures")),
   989	    ),
   990	    toDetailItem(
   991	      "Flooring",
   992	      formatList(getRaw(property, "flooring", "Flooring")),
   993	    ),
   994	    toDetailItem(
   995	      "Construction",
   996	      formatList(getRaw(property, "construction_materials", "ConstructionMaterials")),
   997	    ),
   998	    toDetailItem("Appliances", formatList(getRaw(property, "appliances", "Appliances"))),
   999	  ]);
  1000	
  1001	  pushSection("utilities_services", "Utilities & Services", [
  1002	    toDetailItem("Utilities", formatList(getRaw(property, "utilities", "Utilities"))),
  1003	    toDetailItem(
  1004	      "Water Source",
  1005	      formatList(getRaw(property, "water_source", "WaterSource")),
  1006	    ),
  1007	    toDetailItem("Sewer", formatList(getRaw(property, "sewer", "Sewer"))),
  1008	    toDetailItem("Electric", formatList(getRaw(property, "electric", "Electric"))),
  1009	  ]);
  1010	
  1011	  pushSection("parking_structure", "Parking & Structure", [
  1012	    toDetailItem("Parking", getParkingSummary(property)),
  1013	    toDetailItem(
  1014	      "Parking Features",
  1015	      formatList(getRaw(property, "parking_features", "ParkingFeatures")),
  1016	    ),
  1017	    toDetailItem(
  1018	      "Structure Type",
  1019	      formatList(getRaw(property, "structure_type", "StructureType")),
  1020	    ),
  1021	    toDetailItem(
  1022	      "Property Attached",
  1023	      toValue(getRaw(property, "property_attached_yn", "PropertyAttachedYN")),
  1024	    ),
  1025	  ]);
  1026	
  1027	  pushSection("listing_details", "Listing Details", [
  1028	    toDetailItem(
  1029	      "Postal Code",
  1030	      toValue(getRaw(property, "postal_code", "PostalCode")),
  1031	    ),
  1032	    toDetailItem(
  1033	      "Photos Count",
  1034	      toValue(getRaw(property, "photos_count", "PhotosCount")),
  1035	    ),
  1036	    toDetailItem(
  1037	      "Rooms Total",
  1038	      toValue(
  1039	        (property.rooms || property.Rooms || []).length ||
  1040	          getRaw(property, "total_rooms", "rooms_total", "rooms", "Rooms"),
  1041	      ),
  1042	    ),
  1043	    toDetailItem(
  1044	      "Zoning",
  1045	      toValue(getRaw(property, "zoning_description", "ZoningDescription", "zoning", "Zoning")),
  1046	    ),
  1047	    toDetailItem(
  1048	      "Publish Status",
  1049	      toValue(getRaw(property, "publish_status", "PublishStatus")),
  1050	    ),
  1051	    toDetailItem(
  1052	      "Property ID",
  1053	      toValue(getRaw(property, "property_id_code", "PropertyIdCode")),
  1054	    ),
  1055	    toDetailItem(
  1056	      "Price Prefix",
  1057	      toValue(getRaw(property, "price_prefix", "PricePrefix")),
  1058	    ),
  1059	    toDetailItem(
  1060	      "Second Price",
  1061	      formatCurrency(getRaw(property, "second_price", "SecondPrice")),
  1062	    ),
  1063	  ]);
  1064	
  1065	  const customBlocks = normalizePropertyCustomDetailBlocks(
  1066	    (property as Record<string, unknown>).custom_detail_blocks_json,
  1067	  ).map((block): PropertyDetailSection => ({
  1068	    id: block.id,
  1069	    kind: "custom",
  1070	    title: block.title,
  1071	    items: block.items,
  1072	  }));
  1073	  const layout = normalizePropertyDetailBlockLayout(
  1074	    (property as Record<string, unknown>).detail_blocks_layout_json,
  1075	  );
  1076	
  1077	  if (customBlocks.length === 0 && layout.length === 0) {
  1078	    return sections;
  1079	  }
  1080	
  1081	  const sectionMap = new Map<string, PropertyDetailSection>();
  1082	  [...sections, ...customBlocks].forEach((section) => {
  1083	    if (section.id) sectionMap.set(section.id, section);
  1084	  });
  1085	
  1086	  const ordered: PropertyDetailSection[] = [];
  1087	  const used = new Set<string>();
  1088	  for (const item of layout) {
  1089	    if (!item.visible) {
  1090	      used.add(item.id);
  1091	      continue;
  1092	    }
  1093	    const section = sectionMap.get(item.id);
  1094	    if (!section) continue;
  1095	    ordered.push(section);
  1096	    used.add(item.id);
  1097	  }
  1098	
  1099	  const appendMissing = (section: PropertyDetailSection) => {
  1100	    if (!section.id || used.has(section.id)) return;
  1101	    ordered.push(section);
  1102	    used.add(section.id);
  1103	  };
  1104	  sections.forEach(appendMissing);
  1105	  customBlocks.forEach(appendMissing);
  1106	
  1107	  return ordered;
  1108	};
  1109	
  1110	export const getFormattedRoomDimensions = (room: Record<string, unknown>): string => {
  1111	  const direct = toValue(room.room_dimensions ?? room.RoomDimensions);
  1112	  if (direct) return direct;
  1113	
  1114	  const length = toValue(room.room_length ?? room.RoomLength);
  1115	  const width = toValue(room.room_width ?? room.RoomWidth);
  1116	  const units = toValue(room.room_length_width_units ?? room.RoomLengthWidthUnits);
  1117	
  1118	  if (length && width) {
  1119	    return units ? `${length} x ${width} ${units}` : `${length} x ${width}`;
  1120	  }
  1121	  return "";
  1122	};

FILE: frontend/lib/formatters.ts
================================================================
     1	/**
     2	 * Centralized formatting utilities to ensure consistency across the application.
     3	 * Forces 'en-US' locale to prevent hydration mismatches.
     4	 */
     5	
     6	export function formatCurrency(value: number | string): string {
     7	    const numericValue = typeof value === "string" ? parseFloat(value) : value;
     8	
     9	    if (isNaN(numericValue)) return "Price on request";
    10	
    11	    return `$${numericValue.toLocaleString("en-US", {
    12	        minimumFractionDigits: 0,
    13	        maximumFractionDigits: 0,
    14	    })}`;
    15	}
    16	
    17	export function formatNumber(value: number | string): string {
    18	    const numericValue = typeof value === "string" ? parseFloat(value) : value;
    19	
    20	    if (isNaN(numericValue)) return "0";
    21	
    22	    return numericValue.toLocaleString("en-US");
    23	}
    24	
    25	export function formatArea(value: number | string, unit: string = "sqft"): string {
    26	    const formattedNumber = formatNumber(value);
    27	    return `${formattedNumber} ${unit}`;
    28	}

================================================================
FILE: frontend/hooks/useOneRowListing.ts
================================================================
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import { useState, useEffect } from "react";
     4	import type { Property } from "@/lib/api";
     5	import {
     6	  HOMEPAGE_ROW_COUNT_EVENT,
     7	  HOMEPAGE_ROW_COUNT_PREF_KEY,
     8	  parseHomepageRowCountPreference,
     9	} from "@/lib/homepage/rowPreference";
    10	
    11	/**
    12	 * useOneRowListing Hook
    13	 *
    14	 * Provides "Intelligent Delta-Fetching" logic for homepage sections that only show one row.
    15	 * Automatically handles screen breakpoints, delta-fetching to avoid over-fetching,
    16	 * and caching of previously fetched items.
    17	 *
    18	 * @param fetchFn The API function to call. Must accept { limit, offset }.
    19	 * @param dependencies Optional array of state that should trigger a full reset (e.g., province changes).
    20	 */
    21	export function useOneRowListing(
    22	  fetchFn: (params: {
    23	    limit: number;
    24	    offset: number;
    25	  }) => Promise<{ results: any[]; count: number }>,
    26	  dependencies: any[] = [],
    27	) {
    28	  const [properties, setProperties] = useState<Property[]>([]);
    29	  const [totalCount, setTotalCount] = useState(0);
    30	  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
    31	  const [isError, setIsError] = useState(false);
    32	  const [requestedCount, setRequestedCount] = useState(0);
    33	  const [preferredCount, setPreferredCount] = useState<number | null>(null);
    34	
    35	  useEffect(() => {
    36	    if (typeof window === "undefined") return;
    37	
    38	    const sync = () => {
    39	      const raw = window.localStorage.getItem(HOMEPAGE_ROW_COUNT_PREF_KEY);
    40	      setPreferredCount(parseHomepageRowCountPreference(raw));
    41	    };
    42	
    43	    sync();
    44	    window.addEventListener(HOMEPAGE_ROW_COUNT_EVENT, sync);
    45	    window.addEventListener("storage", sync);
    46	    return () => {
    47	      window.removeEventListener(HOMEPAGE_ROW_COUNT_EVENT, sync);
    48	      window.removeEventListener("storage", sync);
    49	    };
    50	  }, []);
    51	
    52	  // 1. Breakpoint Sensor
    53	  useEffect(() => {
    54	    const calculateRequired = () => {
    55	      if (typeof window === "undefined") return 4;
    56	      const width = window.innerWidth;
    57	
    58	      // BREAKPOINTS SYNCED WITH tailwind.config.ts & PropertyGridSection.tsx:
    59	      // sm=640, md=768, lg=1024, 2xl=1536, 3xl=1800, 4xl=2200
    60	      if (width >= 2200) return 12; // 4xl
    61	      if (width >= 1800) return 8;  // 3xl
    62	      if (width >= 1536) return 6;  // 2xl
    63	      if (width >= 1024) return 4;  // lg + xl (1024–1535px)
    64	      if (width >= 768) return 3;  // md
    65	      if (width >= 640) return 2;  // sm
    66	      return 2;                     // mobile
    67	    };
    68	
    69	    const applyPreference = (autoCount: number) => {
    70	      if (preferredCount && preferredCount > 0) {
    71	        return Math.min(autoCount, preferredCount);
    72	      }
    73	      return autoCount;
    74	    };
    75	
    76	    setRequestedCount(applyPreference(calculateRequired()));
    77	
    78	    const handleResize = () => {
    79	      const needed = calculateRequired();
    80	      setRequestedCount(applyPreference(needed));
    81	    };
    82	
    83	    window.addEventListener("resize", handleResize);
    84	    return () => window.removeEventListener("resize", handleResize);
    85	  }, [preferredCount]);
    86	
    87	  // 2. Clear cache when dependencies change (e.g. search query or province)
    88	  useEffect(() => {
    89	    setProperties([]);
    90	    setTotalCount(0);
    91	    setIsLoading(true);
    92	    setIsError(false);
    93	  }, dependencies);
    94	
    95	  // 3. Intelligent Delta-Fetching
    96	  useEffect(() => {
    97	    // Wait for sensor to determine visible count
    98	    if (requestedCount === 0) return;
    99	
   100	    // Cache guard: Don't fetch if we already have enough items for this row width
   101	    if (properties.length >= requestedCount) {
   102	      return;
   103	    }
   104	
   105	    const fetchDelta = async () => {
   106	      // Only show initial loading state if we have no data yet
   107	      if (properties.length === 0) {
   108	        setIsLoading(true);
   109	      }
   110	
   111	      try {
   112	        const offset = properties.length;
   113	        const limitNeeded = requestedCount - offset;
   114	
   115	        const response = await fetchFn({
   116	          limit: limitNeeded,
   117	          offset: offset,
   118	        });
   119	
   120	        const newProperties = response.results || [];
   121	        setProperties((prev) => [...prev, ...newProperties]);
   122	        setTotalCount(response.count || 0);
   123	      } catch (error) {
   124	        console.error("Error in useOneRowListing Intelligent Fetching:", error);
   125	        setIsError(true);
   126	      } finally {
   127	        setIsLoading(false);
   128	      }
   129	    };
   130	
   131	    fetchDelta();
   132	    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
   133	  }, [requestedCount, ...dependencies]);
   134	
   135	  return {
   136	    properties,
   137	    totalCount,
   138	    isLoading,
   139	    isError,
   140	    requestedCount,
   141	  };
   142	}

================================================================
FILE: frontend/hooks/useProvinceProperties.ts
================================================================
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import { useProvince } from "@/contexts/ProvinceContext";
     4	import {
     5	  fetchProperties,
     6	  type PropertyFilterParams,
     7	  type Property,
     8	} from "@/lib/api";
     9	import { useCallback } from "react";
    10	
    11	/**
    12	 * Custom hook that integrates province context with property API calls
    13	 * Ensures all property searches respect the selected province
    14	 */
    15	export function useProvinceProperties() {
    16	  const { selectedProvince, getProvinceName } = useProvince();
    17	
    18	  /**
    19	   * Fetch properties with automatic province filtering
    20	   * @param additionalFilters - Optional additional filters to apply
    21	   * @returns Promise<Property[]>
    22	   */
    23	  const fetchProvinceProperties = useCallback(
    24	    async (
    25	      additionalFilters: Omit<PropertyFilterParams, "province"> = {},
    26	    ): Promise<Property[]> => {
    27	      const provinceName = getProvinceName(selectedProvince);
    28	
    29	      const filters: PropertyFilterParams = {
    30	        province: provinceName,
    31	        ...additionalFilters,
    32	      };
    33	
    34	      console.log("Fetching properties with province filter:", filters);
    35	      return fetchProperties(filters);
    36	    },
    37	    [selectedProvince, getProvinceName],
    38	  );
    39	
    40	  /**
    41	   * Get the current province information
    42	   */
    43	  const getCurrentProvince = useCallback(() => {
    44	    return {
    45	      code: selectedProvince,
    46	      name: getProvinceName(selectedProvince),
    47	    };
    48	  }, [selectedProvince, getProvinceName]);
    49	
    50	  return {
    51	    fetchProvinceProperties,
    52	    getCurrentProvince,
    53	    selectedProvince,
    54	    provinceName: getProvinceName(selectedProvince),
    55	  };
    56	}

     1	import { strict as assert } from "node:assert";

     5	describe("buildFilterSearchParams", () => {

     8	      status_group: ["active", "sold", "de-listed"],

    11	  });
    12	
    13	  it("remaps property_sub_type and ignores false booleans", () => {
    14	    const params = buildFilterSearchParams({
    15	      property_sub_type: "Detached",
    16	      has_lease: false,
    17	      has_photos: true,
    18	    });
    19	    assert.equal(params.get("property_type"), "Detached");
    20	    assert.equal(params.get("has_lease"), null);
    21	    assert.equal(params.get("has_photos"), "true");
    22	  });
    23	});

FILE: frontend/lib/api/estate.test.ts

     1	import { strict as assert } from "node:assert";
     2	import { describe, it } from "node:test";
     3	import {
     4	  getEstateProjectLocation,
     5	  getEstateProjectFacts,
     6	  getEstateProjectPriceLabel,
     7	  getEstateProjectUrl,
     8	} from "./estate";
     9	
    10	describe("estate project display helpers", () => {
    11	  it("builds a detail URL from a slug", () => {
    12	    assert.equal(
    13	      getEstateProjectUrl({ id: 12, slug: "my-project" }),
    14	      "/pre-construction/my-project",
    15	    );
    16	  });
    17	
    18	  it("falls back to the numeric ID when the slug is missing", () => {
    19	    assert.equal(
    20	      getEstateProjectUrl({ id: 12, slug: null }),
    21	      "/pre-construction/12",
    22	    );
    23	  });
    24	
    25	  it("joins available location fields and reports a fully missing address", () => {
    26	    assert.equal(
    27	      getEstateProjectLocation({ address: "10 King St", city: "Toronto", province: "ON" }),
    28	      "10 King St, Toronto, ON",
    29	    );
    30	    assert.equal(
    31	      getEstateProjectLocation({ address: null, city: null, province: null }),
    32	      "Address unavailable",
    33	    );
    34	  });
    35	
    36	  it("uses real price text and reports missing pricing honestly", () => {
    37	    assert.equal(
    38	      getEstateProjectPriceLabel({ lowest_price_display: "From $500,000" }),
    39	      "From $500,000",
    40	    );
    41	    assert.equal(
    42	      getEstateProjectPriceLabel({ lowest_price_display: null }),
    43	      "Contact for pricing",
    44	    );
    45	  });
    46	
    47	  it("omits missing developer and occupancy facts", () => {
    48	    assert.deepEqual(
    49	      getEstateProjectFacts({ developer: null, occupancy_year: null }),
    50	      [],
    51	    );
    52	    assert.deepEqual(
    53	      getEstateProjectFacts({ developer: "Example Homes", occupancy_year: 2028 }),
    54	      [
    55	        { label: "Developer", value: "Example Homes" },
    56	        { label: "Occupancy", value: "2028" },
    57	      ],
    58	    );
    59	  });
    60	});
